(November 16th)

Xuwan Is Again Under Bandit Attack - This Battle Is of Great Importance to the Future of Bandit Suppression - All Circles Send 10,000 Yuan to Fuzhou to Reward the Troops

Nanchang correspondence: The battle of Xuwan in the Northern Route Army is of paramount importance to the overall situation in Eastern Jiangxi and the safety of Fuzhou. After the desperate and bloody battles of the Fourth Division and the Thirty-sixth Division, the main force of the false Third and Seventh Army Corps was completely defeated, and Fuzhou turned from danger to safety, which is indeed a fortunate event.

Earlier, the bandits used the false 15th Army Corps to contain the southeastern forces of the Northern Route Bandit Suppression Army in Lichuan, Nancheng, and Nanfeng, and secretly had Peng Dehuai of the false Third Army Corps and Fang Zhimin of the false Seventh Army Corps sneak into Jinxi. Fearing airplanes, they moved by night, desperately attacking westward, vainly hoping to bypass the rear of the National Army and seize Fuzhou. The bandits used the false 19th and 20th Divisions as the vanguard. After occupying Jinxi, they advanced to the vicinity of Fengshanbu, south of Xuwan, on the 10th. It was found that Xuwan was an important town on the border between Qianchuan and Jinxi, only forty li from Fuzhou. The National Army had long placed heavy troops here to block them. When the bandits attacked Fengshanbu, they were defeated by the National Army. Unexpectedly, the bandits received reinforcements on the 12th and counterattacked Xuwan extremely fiercely. The National Army, the Song Xilian's troops dispatched from Fuzhou, fought a bloody battle with the bandits near Xuwan. The flames of war filled the sky, and stray bullets rained down. At that time, the bandits were trying to enter Fuzhou in one fell swoop. Just then, Commander-in-Chief Gu had telegraphed and transferred Xing Zhendong's southern troops from Guixi to Jinxi to attack the bandits' rear and reinforce Xuwan. Division Commander Xing led about three regiments of troops, advancing towards Xuwan via Langju, taking a pincer-like formation with Song's division. At about 1:00 PM on the 12th, Division Commander Xing arrived near Daxiangling in Wugang, south of Xuwan, and built a simple fortification there for cover. At 3:00 PM, he attacked the bandits on Daxuling, but because the bandits had already built fortifications on the ridge, several attacks were unsuccessful, so he temporarily took a defensive posture, confronting the bandits on Daxiangling. However, when the false 19th and 20th Divisions attacked Xuwan, Zhu De and Mao Zedong believed that the National Army would definitely have troops bypassing their rear to reinforce Xuwan, so they pre-emptively ambushed the false 4th, 5th, 6th Divisions, and the New Third Division near Langju. When Division Commander Xing opened Xuwan, they secretly followed behind. Starting at 7:00 PM, the false 4th, 5th, and 6th Divisions began to attack the rear of Division Commander Xing, taking a encircling formation with the false 19th and 20th Divisions. Division Commander Xing was surrounded on all sides in the dark night, but he calmly responded to the battle, standing firm as a mountain. The bandits used close-order formations of platoons and companies to launch fierce attacks, no less than ten times. Division Commander Xing waited until they were close, then opened fire with machine guns, grenades, and rifles, as dense as a string of firecrackers. The bandits fell one after another, like moths to a flame. The corpses in front of the battle formed a meat wall and corpse垒, reaching higher than people. By the morning of the 13th, National Army planes arrived in groups and bombed the bandits fiercely. At that time, the National Army soldiers were even more invigorated and finally repelled the surrounding bandits. The remnants of the false 19th, 4th, 5th, 6th, and Newly Compiled Third Divisions retreated in separate routes towards Liuligang, Langju, and Zixi. According to the telegraph from the headquarters of the Northern Route Army, more than 4,000 bandits were killed in this battle, and more than 800 guns, as well as more than 100 flower machine guns and automatic guns, were captured. Yesterday, someone from Fuzhou said that the battle of Xuwan was indeed extremely fierce, and corpses can still be seen everywhere, constantly catching the eye. Many villages near Xuwan were burned by the bandits, and the houses in Xuwan Town were also damaged, with smoke, dust, tiles, and rubble creating an extremely tragic scene. At this moment, the bandits have retreated to the east of Jinxi and Zixi.

The Jiangxi various circles Association for Allied Bandit Suppression, considering that Song and Xing's divisions risked their lives to kill the enemy and broke the general psychology of fearing bandits, which is of great importance to the future of bandit suppression, specially spent 10,000 yuan yesterday to rush to Fuzhou to reward the troops. (November 16th)

Sichuan Army Encirclement and Suppression of the Xu Bandits - Wang and Fan's Troops Advance Northward - Tian and Deng Discuss and Decide on Troop Deployment Routes - Supervising Commissioners Assist in Military Affairs

Hankou correspondence: The bandit suppression military affairs in Sichuan have been hampered by the inability of various armies to agree on a unified approach, resulting in the growth of bandit power. The bandits occupy the dangerous terrain of the Bashan Mountains and control the source of the Jiaqu River. More than a dozen counties in northern Sichuan have either been swallowed whole or nibbled away. After the fall of Suiding, the situation has become even more serious. Liu Xiang then sent his direct line troops, led by Wang Lingji and Fan Shaozeng, to attack from Liang Kai. Wang and Fan had participated in bandit suppression in western Hubei and had considerable experience. After departing, they engaged in fierce battles with the main force of the Xu bandits between Suiding and Kaijiang, at Mug铺, Pujia Chang, Fenghuang Mountain, Caojiezhe, Sanhuikou, Baibaizi, Huilong Chang, Yongxing Chang, Sanqingsi, Baoding Zhai, Changliuye, Jigongliang, Jiaxi Bridge, and Cutongpu. They repeatedly inflicted heavy casualties on the bandits. The bandits, unable to advance eastward, abandoned Suijing and guarded the Luojiang Estuary, which is a key passage between Sui and Xuan, with all their strength. Liu Xiang, seeing that the advance and suppression by these two troops was going smoothly, ordered them to continue advancing northward to recover Xuanhan. He also urged the four routes of Yang Sen, Li Qixiang, Tian Songyao, and Deng Xihou to advance separately according to the predetermined plan, and used Tang Shizun's troops as the general reserve force, preparing for a major mobilization. Currently, the vanguards of Wang and Fan have reached the Luojiang Estuary and are continuing to fight a bloody battle with the bandits. The headquarters of the five routes has moved from Liangshan to Kaijiang. The troops stationed in Liang Kai have all moved forward. The two routes of Yang Sen and Li Qixiang attacked from Quxian and Yingshan. Liu Cunhou's remnants, after being reorganized by Liu Bangjun, are also awaiting orders to assist in the suppression. As for Tian Songyao and Deng Xihou's two routes, they are responsible for the western side. Tian's troops still guard the left bank of the Jialing River, and Deng's troops have crossed Zitong. Tian and Deng recently met in Huluxi and have decided on the troop deployment routes. After Deng's troops are concentrated in Zhaohua, they will jointly develop eastward. In view of the above situation, the encirclement by various armies is imminent. However, there is still cause for concern. The bandits' military strategy has always been to avoid the strong and attack the weak. The strengths and weaknesses of the various armies are already well understood, so future surprise attacks to the east and west will be even more unpredictable in their intentions. Among the various armies, except for Wang and Fan's two routes, which are advancing victoriously, Yang Sen and others have suffered repeated setbacks and have long feared the bandits like tigers. If they are taken advantage of, the entire military operation will inevitably suffer a setback. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is extremely concerned about the communist disaster in Sichuan. He recently sent Yang Deyuan, Chen Xingya, Yu Kedong, Wang Xiangting, Lei Biao, Li Anzhi, Li Leifu, and other seven people as Sichuan Bandit Suppression Supervising Commissioners to assist Liu Xiang in handling the military affairs of the advance and suppression. Yang and others arrived in Hankou on the 15th, and because they received a telegram order from Chairman Chiang, when they arrived in Hankou, they should first request instructions from He Chengjun, the Pacification Director stationed in Hubei, before entering Sichuan. He Chengjun had gone to Jiangxi, causing a conflict, and they plan to wait for He to return to Hankou before setting off westward. As for the central government sending troops to Sichuan, it is heard that there was such a proposal long ago, and there was talk of transferring a certain unit there. It is recently rumored that Yang Hucheng's troops will open up northern Sichuan, which should be realized. In addition, when the various armies in Sichuan heard that the central government was sending personnel to assist in the suppression, their morale was greatly boosted. (17th)

He Jian Requests Rescission of Tan Changkai's Disciplinary Action; Pingdian Bureau Requests Reconsideration from the Capital; Otherwise, Telegraph Approval for Delayed Execution

Changsha Correspondence: Tan Changkai initially served as a member of the Hunan Provincial Party Headquarters. Because he devoted himself to He Jian's party affairs effectively, He recommended him to the Central Government, who appointed him as a member of the Hunan Provincial Government and concurrently the Director of the Construction Bureau, making him prominent for a time. However, this also laid the foundation for his misfortune. Because Hunan party affairs were deeply affected by the tide of factionalism, Tan became incompatible with the opposing faction. It is said that Tan was initially ordered by the Central Government to withdraw from the Provincial Party Headquarters, and then dismissed from his concurrent position as the Director of the Construction Bureau, all related to factional struggles. Recently, the National Government's Committee for the Discipline of Political Officials issued Judgment No. 10, "Tan Changkai is dismissed from his post and barred from holding office for ten years." Thus, Tan's only remaining position as a member of the Provincial Government was also removed, completely destroying Tan's political life. He Jian, considering Tan as someone who had worked hard for him, specially telegraphed Chairman Lin and President Wang from the Pingxiang Military Camp, requesting the rescission of the case of disciplining Tan, or requesting a delay in execution to allow for appeal. He also ordered Tan Changkai himself to go to the capital to defend himself within a specified time. He's telegram read as follows: "To Chairman Lin of the National Government and President Wang of the Executive Yuan, for your review, member of the Provincial Government Tan Changkai, during his tenure as Director of the Construction Bureau, was impeached for selling sulfur ore. After deliberation by the Committee for the Discipline of Political Officials, a disciplinary action was decided. However, upon investigation of the reasons cited in the decision, in terms of the law, the power to reserve and prohibit exploration and mining as stipulated by the Mining Law is a central authority. However, the Central Government has not issued any orders to the Bureau. Moreover, the Provincial Government had consulted the Ministry of Finance regarding the strict prohibition of exports of various military-related minerals, and the Ministry of Finance replied that the opinions of the Ministry of Military Administration advocated detailed research, while the Ministry of Industry and Commerce stated that an absolute prohibition on exports would inevitably have a significant impact on the mining industry, and should continue to be handled as before, except that after the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has a reliable method of maintaining the mining industry, it will be re-evaluated before the prohibition is implemented. Furthermore, in terms of the facts, the official did not directly or indirectly sell ore to aid the enemy during his tenure in the Construction Bureau. As for issuing shipping manifests, it was for the convenience of the Central Government in collecting mineral taxes, which has not been stopped to this day. The situation in other provinces is also the same. Moreover, the official stated in detail in his petition to the Disciplinary Committee, but it was not considered, and a severe penalty was hastily imposed, which seems unfair. In addition to the official's appeal, I respectfully request that it be submitted for reconsideration, rescinding the disciplinary action, or otherwise, please approve a delay in execution to allow for appeal and to demonstrate justice. Respectfully, He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government."

He Jingcheng in Western Hunan Colludes with Border Bandits and Makes Disturbances; Declares Himself Commander of the "All-People National Salvation Army of the Republic of China"; Occupies Jingzhou and Suining Areas, Changes to the Five-Colored Flag

Changsha Correspondence: The Yuanjiang, Jingzhou, and Hongjiang areas of western Hunan were occupied by Chen Wo, Liao Xiangyun, Yan Zhongru, etc., in May of this year. He Jian dispatched three brigades of troops or more, including those of Chen Zixian, Li Guojun, and Xie Long, to defeat them. He Jian then appointed Li Jue, the commander of the 19th Division, as the commander of the Fourth Security Zone, stationed in Hongjiang. He also appointed Peng Zhuo as the Director of the Xiangxi Rehabilitation Office, intending to use military force to advance politics and ensure that the Provincial Government's policies reached the counties of Yuanjiang and Jingzhou. Unexpectedly, before the Rehabilitation Office was established, He Jingcheng, the commander of the First Regiment of the Fourth Security Zone, led his troops, composed of Xiangxi natives from the Gelaohui secret society, in a disturbance. He had been recruited and incorporated as a regimental commander by He Jian. Recently, He Jian ordered He's troops to go to Pingli and Liuyang to suppress bandits, but He was uneasy, and his troops were unwilling to leave their base. Therefore, he openly colluded with border bandits from Hunan and Guizhou, occupying the Jing County and Suining area, calling themselves the "All-People National Salvation Army of the Republic of China", changing to the Five-Colored Flag, and promoting Yu Yizhong as the commander-in-chief, He Jingcheng as the commander of the First Division, someone (name unknown) as the commander of the Second Division, and Lu Xin (who once served as the commander of bandit suppression in the Hunan-Guizhou border area) as the commander of the Third Division. They also declared that they would attack Hongjiang. It is said that Chen Wo, Liao Xiangyun, Yan Zhongru, etc., who are lurking on the Guizhou border, will also make a comeback and cooperate with He, etc. The intentions of the so-called All-People National Salvation Army are still unclear to the province. However, most of the provincial army has already gone to Jiangxi to suppress bandits, and cannot be transferred to western Hunan at present. Therefore, they have only instructed Chen Zixian, etc., to temporarily take a defensive position and stay in Hongjiang to observe the situation. It seems that the Xiangxi area is again in trouble. (November 16)

Liu Zhi Tours Northern Henan; First Goes to Hua County to Inspect the Flood; Then Goes to the Wu'an and She County Area

Kaifeng Correspondence: Liu Zhi originally planned to tour the Wu'an and She County areas on the morning of the 14th to inspect the administration of officials. Therefore, he appointed his entourage and prepared to depart on the 13th. Unexpectedly, the north wind was harsh, and the drizzle was misty, and it did not stop until late at night. He then decided to depart after the rain cleared and the sky cleared, and sent letters to the Henan Civil News and the Republic Daily to disclose the news of the rescheduled tour. This morning, the weather was quite good. Mr. Liu, accompanied by Secretary Li Zhenfeng, staff member Xue Shirong of the First Section, staff member Zhang Faquan of the Second Section, staff member Wang Tingkai of the Third Section, staff member Wang Yimin of the Fourth Section, and more than twenty other people, took a special train to Zhengzhou around 8:00 am, then transferred to the Pinghan Railway to northern Henan. He first went to Hua County to inspect the flood, and then went to the Wu'an and She County area to inspect the administration of officials. He is expected to return to Bian in about a week. (November 15)

Financial Panic in Xuzhou; Paper Money of Various Private Banks Experiences Runs; County Government Clears Paper Money of Various Private Banks

Xuzhou Correspondence: Since the simultaneous runs on the paper money of seven private banks, including Xu Bu's Gongyu, began on the 11th, a huge wave has been stirred up in Xuzhou's financial circles. Up to now, for a week, the market is still in a state of panic. Even the towns closer to Xuzhou have been affected. Because private paper money has no guarantee and no reserve fund, business has been sluggish and finance has been tight in recent years. Although the various private banks have some real estate, it is difficult to mortgage for cash. Moreover, the assets of each individual are not enough to offset the amount of paper money they have issued. Therefore, although the county government presides over maintaining the status quo on the one hand and thoroughly clearing on the other, it is ultimately unable to take effective measures due to insufficient credit and lack of cash. Those who run continue to run, and those who refuse to use it refuse to use it. The panic in the market remains the same. According to the amount of paper money and the amount of property reported by the various private banks, Gongyu has issued 700,000 strings of cash, with real estate on Yinshi Street worth 20,000 yuan and accounts receivable worth 40,000 yuan. At a rate of five strings per silver yuan, the equivalent of 140,000 yuan was issued, while the real estate and accounts receivable can only offset 60,000 yuan. Because it is a shareholder business, manager Zhang Shaozhi cannot maintain it. The county government convened a meeting of shareholders yesterday, but there were no results. It is now planned to have the shareholders guarantee and borrow money from the bank to clear the debt. However, at this time of extreme financial crisis, the bank also does not have so much money to use. As for the other companies, the manager of Chuanquan Store, Zhang Zuiping, has issued 500,000 strings of cash, with property consisting of land in Yuzhuang and Gushan, totaling 20 hectares, valued at 80,000 yuan, but only 10 hectares are held by the title, accounts receivable of 40,000 yuan, and only 3,000 yuan in cash. The manager of Shixingchang Store, Zhang Jingxiu, has issued 250,000 strings of cash, with real estate in Zhou Dong Lane worth 4,000 yuan, 3.9 hectares of land worth 34,000 yuan, accounts receivable of 20,000 yuan, and only 4,000 yuan in cash. The owner of Tianbaoyu Store, Zhao Bangqing, has issued 200,000 strings of cash, with real estate and land worth a total of 34,000 yuan, and accounts receivable of 20,000 yuan. The owner of Buxinji Store, Bu Zhiping, has issued 170,000 strings of cash, with real estate on Daoping Road worth 10,000 yuan, on Fushui Well worth 12,000 yuan, and on Bazi Street worth 20,000 yuan, and only 3,000 yuan in cash. The owner of Juhechang Store, Wang Fuqing, has issued 160,000 strings of cash, with real estate in Ma Hao Town worth 3,000 yuan, 1.5 hectares of land worth 9,000 yuan, an educational loan of 800 yuan, goods worth 4,000 yuan, and accounts receivable of 20,000 yuan. The owner of Yizhenxiang Store, Ding Yinzhou, has issued 100,000 strings of cash, with three mu of real estate land belonging to the Longhai Road, with ten buildings and seventy-two flat houses, with a construction cost of 21,000 yuan, of which a part has been used to guarantee credit for 1,700 yuan, and the accounts receivable are not detailed on a separate sheet. According to this, the amount of paper money and property reported by the various private banks can be offset, but the value of the property varies greatly, and a discount must be applied for mortgage, so the actual calculation is still not enough.

In recent days, in addition to the paper money panic in the local area, nearby areas have also reported alarms at the same time. For example, in Huangkou, the seven private currencies of Shaoyou Gongyu, etc., amount to as much as 150,000 yuan. Huangkou is demanding that the Commissioner's Office of the 12th District order the various private banks to bring money to Huangkou to redeem them, but the local area is still unable to maintain them, let alone have the capacity to reach the outer areas. Moreover, most of the banknotes issued by the various banks are used to purchase agricultural products for the purpose of transporting and mortgaging cash, resulting in even more banknotes being stored in the countryside. If they are fundamentally bankrupt, social order will be in jeopardy. County Magistrate She is using the assets of each company to negotiate with the banking sector to offset cash, ordering them to clean up separately, and is planning to convene a county consolidation committee, district office, chamber of commerce, and money industry association to organize a committee to clean up private banknotes to seek a thorough resolution. The County Consolidation Committee also convened various agencies and groups yesterday to discuss solutions, and decided to telegraph the province to send a commissioner to Xuzhou to thoroughly supervise the cleanup to eliminate the harm of banknotes. It is hoped that the disaster of Xuzhou banknotes can be cleared. However, the market is currently sluggish, the rural areas are bankrupt, and ordinary poor farmers do not have small businesses to operate, and most of them have unredeemable banknotes that cannot be circulated. If they cannot be redeemed in the future, the losers will be ordinary people, which is worrying. The crowded scene at the public exchange is mostly controlled by gangsters, who redeem them at a discount. Redeem one yuan of cash and only recover nine cents. Village women and children come to the city after running dozens of miles, and all return with tears, which is really sad to see. Those responsible should design more for these poor people. At this critical time of collapse of Xuzhou banknotes, the current maintenance and thorough cleanup must be considered together, aiming at stabilizing the current society and permanently eliminating future disasters. It is also the entire social problem of Xuzhou, which the people expect. (November 17)

Suzhou

Streamlining and Merging of Provincial Water Police

In order to reorganize the provincial water police, Commissioner Gu of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Office plans to merge the six districts in the province into three districts, and the ten detachments into four detachments, and eliminate one-third of the old and weak police officers. The Wu County Commercial, Agricultural and Educational organizations, considering that this is during the winter defense period, have sent telegrams to the provincial office, requesting a delay in the merger. In addition, Wei Zhanyuan, the District Chief of the Third Water Police District, was summoned to the province by Commissioner Gu yesterday to discuss the streamlining and merger matters. As for the issuance of back pay, the province is planning and hopes to issue it soon.

Kunshan

Robbers of the Gonghe Pawnshop Arrested

Around 1:00 am on the 17th, the Gonghe Pawnshop in Zhengyi Town was suddenly entered by eight or nine bandits who dug a hole. After deceiving the pawnshop clerk into a room, they searched and robbed for about an hour before escaping with the loot, estimated to be more than 1,000 yuan in cash and jewelry. After receiving the report, Hua Shijun, the Director of the County Public Security Bureau, immediately ordered Patrol Officer Dai Yuheng to lead the police to guard the Su-Kun Highway. At the same time, he cooperated with Police Captain Luo Qixiang to supervise the police detectives to pursue the escaped bandits by both land and water routes. At 5:30 am, Patrol Officer Dai arrested two bandits, Zhang Yunsheng and Zhang Gansheng, on the Su-Kun Road, and seized a gold ingot, a watch, and 130 yuan in cash on the spot. He immediately escorted them to the bureau for interrogation. The two criminals confessed that they committed the robbery of the Gonghe Pawnshop with Chen A San and Wang A Er. Director Hua immediately prepared a document to transfer them to the county government for legal action.

Taicang

Two Robberies in One Night

In Shaotian, Beixiang, Penglai Town, which belongs to the county, there are about 30 households, all of whom are farmers. The Qian and Yu families are relatively well-off, which has been coveted by bandits. At midnight the day before yesterday, when all the villagers were sound asleep, six or seven robbers suddenly came. They first went to the Qian family, broke down the gate, and broke into the bedroom, searching and robbing clothes and jewelry worth dozens of silver dollars. Then they went to the Yu family to rob, driving the family members into a room, tying them up with ropes, and rummaging through boxes and cabinets, robbing and leaving the land deeds and house receipts. There was no loss of clothes or jewelry. Before leaving, they took away five dan of white rice before leaving.

Fierce Battle between Police and Bandits in Shuangfeng Laoya

The Fourth Water Police District, considering the importance of the defense of Liuhou River, ordered the First Squad of the 16th Brigade under its jurisdiction to be stationed there. Among them, eight police soldiers deserted with weapons last month, joined the bandits, and hid in Shuangfeng Laoya Jiang. Huang, the commander of the Liuhou Security Corps, got a tip the day before yesterday and secretly dispatched three experienced members, Zhou Pin San, Xie De Rong, and Chen Fengqi, with the tipster, to Shaxi. They met with the First Squad of the Fifth Brigade of the First Water Police District. Captain Li Zhigui sent a patrol boat, along with detectives Wang Guozhi and Li Lixiang, to sail to Zhitang to land. They disguised themselves as bandits and, led by the tipster, walked to Zhaojiazhai in Shuangfeng Laoya Jiang, where they pretended to be merchants to do business with the bandits. The bandits sent out two small boats. When the tipster gave a secret signal, the police rushed forward. The two sides exchanged dozens of gunshots, resulting in the capture of four bandits, Wang Zhu San, Yu Cao Qing, Wu Zhi Yuan, and Wang Shi Hong, with the rest escaping. Two rifles and more than 100 rounds of ammunition were seized. The captured bandits were sent to the First Unit for custody. After reporting back to the Corps, they will go to meet and bring them to justice.

Wuxi

Wu Zhihui and Others Inspect Mashan

Wu Zhihui and Niu Yongjian, important figures in the Party and State, considering that Mashan in Taihu Lake is barren and the people are poor, and have suffered for many years, specially went to Xueyanqiao by boat at noon yesterday (the 18th) with Yu Qingtang, Gao Jiansi, and Xue Mingjian, and transferred to a civilian boat to Mashan to inspect the residents' lives and occupations, etc., in order to find ways to provide relief.

Misconduct Discovered in Bail of Criminals

The Wuxi County Prison Improvement Association held its eighth committee meeting yesterday. Chairman Yan Shenyu discussed the following matters: 1. Commissioners Xu Tigan and Zhou Erkai sent a letter stating that there was no Wang Zhenkun in the case of bailing out 36 people, including Huang Ziyu, etc. It is now found that the former prison officer Han reported that the name of the criminal was added to the list of previously bailed criminals. What is the situation? The resolution was to request an investigation into the case. The resolution was that the former prison officer Han added the name of Wang Zhenkun to the list when applying for bail after it had been reviewed. Whether there was any wrongdoing in it should be handed over to the Procuratorate of the County Court for investigation, and a report should be made to the High Court. 2. Commissioner Kong Xian proposed to ask the County Court to temporarily keep prisoners sentenced to short-term detention and those fined for less than one month in the prison for execution in order to facilitate the process. The resolution was to transfer the matter to the Procuratorate of the County Court for review. 3. Commissioner Xu Tigan proposed that the county raised funds to build a prison. How much did the former prison officer Han collect, and how should it be handled since it has not been clearly transferred after handing over the office? The resolution was to urge the former prison officer to quickly transfer the collected donations and the donation booklet. 4. Commissioners Xu and Zhou proposed to take turns sending people to inspect the prison in order to improve it. The resolution was to recommend Commissioner Sun Qing and Commissioner Cheng Jingtang to inspect and submit a written report at the next meeting. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Garment Industry Announces Another Strike

The garment industry in Wuxi filed a petition with the county government to ban the establishment of new garment departments by various silk shops, which encroached on their business, and jointly petitioned the county party headquarters. The situation has been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the county government approved the garment industry a few days ago, stating that the establishment of new garment departments by the silk and satin industry is a matter of business freedom, and the requested ban is difficult to approve. After receiving the approval, the industry was dissatisfied and convened more than 1,000 garment industry workers from inside and outside the city, departing from the guild hall in Shipi Lane to petition the county government. More than a dozen representatives from each district were elected to meet with the county magistrate. County Magistrate Yan sent staff member Zhou Shaoji to receive them and verbally instructed the representatives that the case had been approved and that they should rest assured that they would not act rashly. The representatives did not get what they wanted and withdrew together. However, the members' intentions were extremely firm, and they would not give up until they achieved their goals. Therefore, from the afternoon of the day before yesterday, some garment shops automatically went on strike. From the morning of yesterday (the 18th), more than 1,000 garment shops in the county went on strike to show their determination. At 2:00 pm, Qian Zhanhong, chairman of the Garment Industry Association, invited the heads of the new garment departments of silk and satin shops such as Shitaishing, Shihe, Rixin, Maolun, Jiusheng, and Xieshengyong to the association to negotiate a solution. However, the silk industry believed that the establishment of new garment departments was originally for the purpose of developing business and had nothing to do with the garment industry's business, so it was inconvenient to discuss. The garment industry also submitted a petition to the county chamber of commerce to provide relief and to quickly forward a letter to the silk and cloth industry to convene a meeting with the new garment departments to persuade them not to make Chinese clothing in order to avoid causing opinions among more than 3,000 garment workers. After the petition was sent, there has been no indication so far. A large number of workers are gathered in the association, holding meetings repeatedly, but some workers have different opinions, causing noise and causing small disputes among colleagues. The purpose of the workers' demands in this strike is only to change the name of the new garment department to the Western garment department, and the strike can be resolved. It is also heard that if the silk and satin industry does not make some concessions, the garment industry workers will take further measures to deal with it. One or two hundred people will be assigned to each silk shop to sit and eat to observe the situation, which is quite determined. The strike may expand.

Changzhou

Provincial Party Headquarters Sends a Commissioner to Investigate the Suicide Case

Lin You'e, the accountant of the Lihua Cotton Weaving Factory in Wu Yi, was detained by the Public Security Bureau for the Anti-Japanese Association's case of hatred for yarn. After Lin hanged himself in custody, the Provincial Party Headquarters, upon receiving the report, specially sent Commissioner Duan Benzhen to Changzhou to investigate. Duan first went to the Public Security Bureau, where he was received by Section Chief Si Daoping, who reported on Lin You'e's detention and suicide. Commissioner Duan resigned and then went to the Procuratorate of the County Court to investigate, where he was received by Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongxi. In the evening, he met with Lin's family and the managers of the Lihua Factory, Liu Dacai and Yang Shaozhen, at the Dacheng Hotel. On the 16th, Duan left Changzhou to return to the province to report.

Yangzhou

Cook Steals Huge Amount of Money for Buying Grain

On the 17th, Zheng Dayuan, a grain trading firm in Sanhe, had a customer from Zhenjiang, Xiao Huanan, who brought thousands of yuan to the firm to purchase various grains on his behalf. Unexpectedly, around 1:00 am that night, more than 2,000 yuan of the money Xiao had brought was stolen. Upon inquiry, it was found that it was stolen by the cook Yu Xiao Caizi. Traces of Yu were immediately traced, but he had already fled without a trace. The owner of the firm is closely investigating Yu's whereabouts and has reported to the Public Security Bureau for assistance.

Telegram Requesting Cessation of Yutong's Move Northward

The Jiangdu County Chamber of Commerce, Agricultural Association, Education Association, Lawyers Association, and Newspaper Reporters Association stated that on the 3rd of this month, Shen Xin and other newspapers published that Jinan Yutong Company was moving north to Chenjiagang, and Envoy Miao Qiujie of Yun arrived in Yangzhou. In talks with various sectors of society, he denied the company's move north, saying that it was a misunderstanding that the company's shareholders had set up an office in Chengang. They specially jointly telegraphed the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Salt Administration, and the Provincial Government, requesting an immediate cessation. The original telegram roughly said that Yangzhou is centered on the salt industry, and the salt industry is based on the seven companies in Jinan. Education, charity, public security, public welfare, and the employees of Twelve Market depend on it directly or indirectly for their livelihood, totaling more than one million people. The newspaper reported that a small number of shareholders of Yutong Company in Jinan held a meeting in Banpu to discuss moving to Chengang. If the other six companies follow suit, all those who rely on it for their livelihood will lose their jobs, and the local security is too important. We urge you to forward the telegram to Envoy Miao of Huaibei and Deputy Transport Envoy Zhou of Huainan, strictly ordering them to stop it in order to maintain the livelihood and security of the people.

Nantong

Aftermath of the Chenqiao Town Robbery

The robbery of Chenqiao Town and the seizure of weapons from the security corps is a major case. The district corps has arrested six key bandits, including Miao Wensui, and escorted them to the county government for interrogation. Their confessions are cunning. Magistrate Cheng believes that it is necessary to personally investigate, so he went to the town on the 17th with Peng Longxiang, the director of the county security corps, and expressed his condolences to the victimized merchants and residents. They also convened a meeting to discuss relief to military, government, and police agencies. In view of the rampant banditry, they divided the joint defense zone and scheduled a meeting on the 23rd at the Tongcheng Provincial Second Security Corps to discuss the methods of stationing guards.

Jiangyin

Robbery and Murder in Zhangqing Township

At around 10:00 pm the day before yesterday, two people dressed in military uniforms suddenly came to the home of Zhao Huichen, a farmer at No. 22, Village 15, Dahuli, Section 5, Zhangqing Township, District 7, and entered to rob, holding a box gun and shooting Zhao Huichen to death. Afterwards, the Yangku Public Security Third Sub-bureau investigated and reported to the headquarters to transfer the county to hunt down the murderers. Magistrate Ruan received the report on the 16th and, as it is now in the winter defense period and rural theft cases are frequent, he strictly ordered his subordinates to strengthen precautions.

Southeast Township School Refuses to Accept

Zhou Fohai, the director of the Department of Education, proposed at the 606th Provincial Government Meeting to concentrate educational property. It was decided that the Department of Education would take over the property of the Southeast and West Townships, and instructed the County Bureau to take over the matter and report it. The Department of Education sent Inspector Hu Chaolun and Chief of General Affairs Qu Yong'e to go to the Southeast Township School on the morning of the 20th to take over. The school specially scheduled a meeting of the board of directors and supervisors at 2:00 pm to discuss countermeasures. It is heard that they completely refused to take over the matter and should argue according to reason and file an appeal with the Ministry of Interior.

Changshu

Fire in Qinglong Lane Injures One Person

The home of a silversmith at No. 4, Qinglong Lane, in the west gate of the town, suddenly caught fire at 7:00 am on the 17th. Because it was still early, it was not noticed at first. It was not until the fire penetrated the roof that passers-by shouted for help. However, the northeast wind was very strong that day. After a while, it spread to the four or five households of the Li family, the Wang family, the Zhou family, and the Gu family on the right and left. After about half an hour, the fire was extinguished by the various fire brigades. This time, six houses and eleven rooms were destroyed, with losses estimated at more than 5,000 yuan. A nearby wealthy household, Zhou Bairen's family, was grateful to the fire brigades for their effective efforts and was not affected. He specially hosted dozens of banquets in the evening to thank the firefighters for their efforts. After the fire, Zhao, a silversmith who lived in the Li Wang Gong Ye Silver Shop, went to watch, but suddenly the dangerous burden collapsed, and Zhao could not avoid it, resulting in serious injuries. He was sent to a trauma clinic in Nanmen for treatment.

Jiashan

Four Robberies in One Night

Bao, a farmer in Hongjia Village, Model Town, Waijiuliwan in the west, is semi-farming and semi-studying, and his family is well-off. Yesterday midnight, more than 40 bandits suddenly came, carrying three bandit ships, and carrying quick guns. They broke down the door and entered the room to rob. They were robbed of 30 dan of white rice and 200 silver yuan. The Zhang and Lu families next door were also affected, and a total of 25 dan of brown rice and other miscellaneous clothes and ornaments were robbed. At the same time, the home of Lao Shanggui, a farmer in Hongdong Port, Qianyao Town, was also robbed of more than 100 yuan of clothes and cash.

County Representatives Request Reorganization of the Bureau of Finance

The County Party Headquarters convened the 14th County Representatives' Conference. The conference stated that the Bureaus of Finance in the provinces and counties were originally the Departments of Finance in the County Governments. During the era of setting up departments, all expenses were paid from the county's administrative expenses. Since the establishment of the Bureau of Finance, the number of staff has increased several times, and the expenses have also increased accordingly. As for this county, in addition to the director, there are also three section chiefs, three clerks, and two secretaries. The expenses have increased from more than 200 yuan to 800 yuan. After the establishment of the Business Tax Bureau, the tooth post tax and slaughter tax, which were originally managed by the Bureau of Finance, were transferred to the Business Tax Bureau. The affairs are simpler than before, but the number of staff is more than before. The contradiction of facts is such that the central government, because the financial situation of Zhejiang Province is difficult, ordered the provincial government that all financial affairs of the Bureau of Finance should still be handled by the County Government setting up a department. Moreover, at this time of serious national crisis and strict austerity, the province should be requested to abolish the Bureau of Finance to avoid wasting public funds. This proposal was passed by the entire body, and a request was immediately submitted to the Provincial Party Headquarters to forward it to the Provincial Government for review.

Funing

The Rampant Banditry in the Southeastern Countryside

Our county borders the sea and has always been known as an area with many bandits. Since the abolition of the four rural public security substations, small-time thieves have taken the opportunity to become more active. In the Huangsha area, just the other day, twelve families were robbed of all their cotton and clothing in one night. All were poor, small households. Last night, over twenty bandits, many carrying electric lights, passed through places like Xiaosha Road and Jiazhuang. They were immediately shot at and pursued by the public, and the bandits returned fire before leaving. Wealthy households nearby are unable to sleep soundly at night and are extremely alarmed.

Rugao

Robbery Occurs in Yuebo Township

In Rugao Shuangdian District, the Gu family in Yuebo Township was suddenly broken into by many bandits on the night of the tenth. They entered the bedroom and fired several shots at the bed, luckily without injuring anyone. It is estimated that over three hundred silver dollars and several pieces of gold jewelry were robbed. The case has now been reported to the county for investigation and arrest.

Female Doctor's Wife Commits Suicide by Swallowing Opium

Kan Xunqing, a doctor in this county, has been practicing medicine for many years and has a small reputation. His family runs a Chinese medicine business, which is doing very well. His wife, Hu, is over forty years old and has a very peaceful nature. She assists with household affairs and keeps everything in good order. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning around eight o'clock, for some unknown reason, she secretly swallowed an ounce of opium and committed suicide. She instructed her daughters-in-law to manage the household affairs well and avoid arguments. After speaking, she lay back on a rattan chair. Her family noticed something was wrong with her expression, and her husband and son tried to rescue her, but to no avail. She died at four o'clock in the afternoon. Her family is overwhelmed with grief, but the reason for her suicide remains unclear.

Hangzhou

Tao Sijin Sent to Prison for Execution

In the case of Tao Sijin, a female student at the West Lake Art Academy, who tragically murdered her classmate Liu Mengying, after the Supreme Court remanded the case for retrial, the Zhejiang High Court sentenced her to life imprisonment and acquitted Xu Qinwen. The prosecutor considered the sentence in this case to be too lenient and appealed to the Supreme Court. However, due to the related Communist Party case involving Song Yuanming, both Xu and Tao were sentenced to five years in prison. Xu was dissatisfied and appealed, but Tao did not appeal. Yesterday (the 18th) at 10:00 AM, the criminal court ordered bailiffs to bring Tao from the Hangzhou County District Court Detention Center and escort her to the First Prison for execution. Tao looked haggard, with tears in her eyes. Her pitiful state was quite heartrending.

Wang Ying's Embezzlement Case Appealed

Wang Ying, the former magistrate of Jiaxing County, embezzled over 90,000 yuan in public funds during his tenure and went into hiding in Shanghai. He was arrested this spring and sent to the Hangzhou Court for trial, where he was sentenced to ten months for embezzlement and ordered to repay the embezzled funds. The prosecutor in this case believed that the sentence was too lenient and filed a public prosecution with the High Court. Yesterday (the 18th) at 3:00 PM, the Second Criminal Division of the High Court brought Wang in for questioning. He was already clear on the details of the case and will be sentenced after summoning witnesses.

Hefei

Primary School Teachers Demand Salary

The teachers and staff of Hefei's primary schools, due to the Education Bureau's significant salary arrears, have repeatedly requested payment without success. They formed a joint association of primary school teachers and staff and negotiated with Cheng Guangshou, the director of the Education Bureau, but to no effect. Director Cheng suddenly went to the provincial capital on the 13th for official business, and the head of the First Section, Lu Shaosan, was delegated to act in his place. The teachers and staff, upon hearing the news, all went to the bus station to demand their salaries from Cheng, nearly resulting in a clash. Cheng stated that Lu was responsible and left. The teachers and staff then went to the Education Bureau to find Lu, but he would not see them. That evening, they decided to strike and announced Cheng's crimes. County Magistrate Guo is currently mediating.

Letter from the Kunshan County Government

To the editor of your esteemed newspaper:

In the "Nanjing News" column of your newspaper on the 18th of this month, there was a report titled "Kunshan Civil Servant Disciplinary Case," which stated that "Kunshan County Magistrate Cheng Ruji violated the law and neglected his duties, and the Control Yuan transferred him to the Disciplinary Committee for disciplinary action according to law." Upon investigation, the original reason for the case transferred by the Control Yuan was that County Magistrate Cheng had illegally harbored subordinates. In July of this year, County Magistrate Cheng submitted a written defense upon the order of the Disciplinary Committee. No disciplinary action has been taken. The newspaper report does not match the case. It concerns the personal reputation of County Magistrate Cheng. Therefore, we are sending the original reason for the case and the facts of the matter, requesting that your newspaper publish them to clarify the truth and avoid misunderstandings. Respectfully, Kunshan County Government, November 18th.

Local News

The National Economic Council Held Its First Regular Meeting Yesterday; Wang Jingwei and Sun Ke Both Came to Shanghai to Attend; It Was Decided to Add Jiang and Kong as Standing Committee Members; Wang and Sun Spoke of the Fujian Disturbance, Believing It Would Not Become a Reality

Premier of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei and President of the Legislative Yuan Sun Ke arrived in Shanghai together yesterday morning by night train from Nanjing, at the invitation of Song Ziwen, to attend the first regular meeting of the Economic Council, to discuss all the ongoing work of the council, and decided to add Chiang, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, and Kong, Minister of Finance, as Standing Committee Members. Regarding the rumored political disturbance brewing in Fujian Province, Wang, Sun, and others all gave speeches, believing that this matter would not become a reality. The details are as follows:

Wang, Sun, and Others Arrive in Shanghai Together

Premier of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei and President of the Legislative Yuan Sun Ke, at the invitation of Song Ziwen, a standing committee member of the Economic Council, came to Shanghai to attend the first regular meeting of the Economic Council to discuss all ongoing work. Those who came to Shanghai with Wang and Sun yesterday morning included Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, Minister of Transportation Zhu Jiahua, Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, and Secretary of the Legislative Yuan Ma Chaojun. They took the night express train from Nanjing together the night before at 11:00 PM. Wang, Zeng, and Chu got off the train at Nanxiang at 7:00 AM, while Sun Ke and Ma Chaojun got off at Zhenru at 7:15 AM. The others got off at the North Station. The Municipal Security Office specially dispatched two teams of soldiers yesterday morning, distributed in Zhenru and the North Station to maintain order.

The Regular Meeting of the Economic Council Was Held Yesterday Morning

The National Economic Council held its first regular meeting of the Standing Committee yesterday morning at 10:00 AM at its Shanghai office located at 1729 Avenue Joffre. The Standing Committee members who attended included Wang Jingwei, Song Ziwen, and Sun Ke. Those attending as observers included Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, Minister of Transportation Zhu Jiahua, and Secretary-General of the Economic Council Qin Fen. At the beginning of the meeting, Song reported on the one-year work plan drafted in Shanghai. Then, the organization of the council and the addition of Standing Committee members were discussed. It was decided to add two more Standing Committee members, and the candidates were already decided: Chiang, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, and Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance. It will be announced after being approved by the Central Political Council next Wednesday. The meeting lasted for three hours and adjourned at 12:40 PM. All the details of the meeting are scheduled to be officially announced at the office on Monday (tomorrow) at 10:00 AM.

Wang Jingwei Discusses the Political Disturbance in Fujian Province

Wang told reporters from various newspapers after the meeting yesterday that this morning, the members of the Economic Council met to discuss the internal organization of the National Economic Council. The Secretary-General, Qin Fen, will be responsible for releasing information about this matter soon. As for the addition of two Standing Committee members, the candidates have been decided as Chiang, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, and Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance. It will be officially announced after being submitted to the Central Political Council for approval next Wednesday. Regarding the brewing of a new organization in Fujian Province, the current situation has gradually eased and is not as serious as the outside world has reported. It is expected that it will not become a reality. The central government believes that it is just a rumor, so it has not prepared to send personnel to mediate. However, if the rumors become a reality, the central government will use political methods to ensure that it is eliminated in its infancy. However, I deeply feel that the country has come to this point, and unity is even more insufficient to resist foreign aggression. How can we further disperse our strength? As for Mr. Hu Zhantang, he is still in Hong Kong, and the central government is eagerly hoping that he will come north to jointly discuss national affairs. Furthermore, the issues of opening traffic and mail in North China are currently not making any real progress. The Japanese side is hoping for negotiations to resolve the issue as soon as possible, but because of the significant impact, we will not proceed rashly without detailed research and consideration.

Sun Zhesheng Talks About Hu Still Being in Hong Kong

Yesterday, the reporter specially drove to visit President of the Legislative Yuan Sun Ke at his private residence to inquire about the truth of the political disturbance in Fujian Province and the mission of this visit. According to him, his purpose in coming to Shanghai today was to participate in the regular meeting of the National Economic Council to discuss all the ongoing work of the council. Regarding the brewing of a new organization in Fujian Province, the central government has not yet received a confirmed report. However, the central government is eagerly hoping that Mr. Hu will come to Nanjing as soon as possible to discuss national affairs. As for the rumor that personnel will be sent to Hong Kong to mediate, it is absolutely not true. The situation in Fujian is still normal, and there is no movement, so there is no need to send personnel.

Zeng and Chu Expressed That Cai and Others Telegraphed Chiang

Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming told reporters yesterday that he came to Shanghai specifically to participate in the naming ceremony of the "Two Roads" aircraft. If this time there is no careful consideration, and changes and internal turmoil occur, causing the local area to be devastated, then the past glory will be destroyed. It is believed that the intelligent and decisive generals of the 19th Route Army will not bear to do this.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sent an Important Telegram Yesterday, Affirming the Principle of Quieting the Interior and Pacifying the Exterior; It Is Necessary to Establish a Direction and Not Be Confused; Everyone Should Fulfill Their Duties and Practice What They Preach

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, due to rumors of unrest in the Fujian political situation, sent a general telegram, making its claims. The original telegram is recorded as follows: Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, all members of the Central Party Headquarters, Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan, Chairman Chiang of Nanchang, all Commanders-in-Chief, Governors of each province, Party Headquarters of each province and city, and Municipal Governments, G鑑, The loss of four provinces and the fragmentation of Hebei, the disturbances in Sichuan and Jiangxi, and the swarming of bandits are all signs that it is easy to talk about quieting the interior and pacifying the exterior in this time of crisis, but difficult to implement. We should first recognize the advantages and disadvantages and not sacrifice the overall plan for the sake of local benefit, so that sovereignty can be secured and lost territories can be recovered. This is the principle of pacifying the exterior. When the country is in distress, discussing major plans can easily lead to disagreements. The idea of縱棧 often leads to opportunities for intervention. This is the source of political instability. This is the principle of quieting the interior. If we ignore this and do not seek improvement, the collapse and disintegration may be unavoidable. The Naming Ceremony of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Aircraft Was Held Yesterday; Wu Tiecheng Was Sent by the Central Government as a Representative to Participate; Shen Dexie Was Sent by the National Government as a Representative to Receive the Aircraft; 50,000 People Went to Hongqiao to Watch the Ceremony; Aviation School Students Performed Amazing Techniques

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo aircraft, purchased by the employees of the "Two Roads" using public welfare funds from the Curtiss Eagle fighter aircraft factory in the United States through the China Aviation Association, held a naming ceremony at the Hongqiao Airport yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. Representatives were sent by both the Central Government and the National Government to participate. The ceremony was very grand. Over 50,000 people from all over the city went to the Hongqiao Airport yesterday to watch the ceremony, making it quite a spectacle. The details are as follows:

Special Trains Were Opened

The "Two Roads" Administration specially opened special trains from the North Station to Xujiahui yesterday. The trains departed from the North Station at 11:55 AM and 1:15 PM. After arriving at the Xujiahui Station, 20 special cars were prepared to drive to the Hongqiao Airport. After the naming ceremony, the special cars drove back from the Hongqiao Airport to the Xujiahui Station and transferred to the special trains departing from Xujiahui at 5:10 PM and 7:00 PM to return to the North Station. The "Two Roads" Air Defense Fundraising Committee issued special publications commemorating the naming of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo aircraft, as well as a letter to the compatriots of the country, colorful leaflets, and slogans, which were all eye-catching.

A Glimpse of the Security

The "Two Roads" Air Defense Fundraising Committee had previously sent a letter to the Security Office of the Garrison Headquarters, as well as various Boy Scout groups, to be responsible for maintaining order at the venue. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, the road from Xujiahui to Hongqiao Airport was guarded by the Public Security Bureau. Around the airport, there were also security offices and airport troops stationed, armed with guns, scattering sentries, and providing strict protection. In addition to the Public Security Bureau's security team protecting the venue, the Boy Scout groups from Moore Hall, the Wu Yu Sports Association, the YMCA, the YMCA Middle School, the Yousheng Travel Group, and other groups also assisted in maintaining order.

Venue Arrangement

At the entrance of the venue, a colorful archway was erected, with a white banner in the middle that read "Naming Ceremony of Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Aircraft." On the side of the venue, a podium was built, with a white banner in the center that also read "Naming Ceremony of Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Aircraft." On both sides were white banners with the couplet "Promoting aviation is the forerunner of saving the country from difficulty," and "Saving the country and resisting foreign aggression must promote the aviation industry." In the center of the stage was a portrait of Sun Yat-sen, with party and national flags crossed on both sides. To the right of the stage, about ten feet away, was the municipal government military band. The surrounding area was surrounded by ropes to prevent the audience from entering, and the Boy Scouts assisted the military and police in maintaining order.

Ms. Tao Chun Throws the Bottle (Photo by Qi Chang)

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony, Chairman Chen Chengshi of the presidium delivered the opening remarks. Then, Yuan Boyang reported on the preparations, stating that the colleagues of the "Two Roads," in view of the importance of aviation in saving the country, in February of this year, the special party headquarters of the "Two Roads" jointly organized the "Two Roads" Air Defense Fundraising Committee with the Administration and the "Two Roads" labor unions to raise funds and prepare an aircraft to donate to the government. After collective discussion by the public welfare committee of the "Two Roads" colleagues, it was decided to allocate the public welfare funds stored by the colleagues for the purchase of the aircraft. Contact was made with the China Aviation Construction Association, and one of the 18 aircraft ordered by the association was transferred. After today's ceremony, it will be presented to the government. We have two hopes: (1) that other railway colleagues will follow suit and donate as much as possible, and (2) that this aircraft will be used effectively for foreign defense in the future, and fight for the glory of the Chinese nation.

After the presidium's report, Mayor Wu (Tiecheng), the representative of the Central Party Headquarters, gave a speech, stating that he was very honored to represent the Central Party Headquarters and participate in today's naming ceremony of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo aircraft. He deeply admired them. Then, Kong Xiangxi, the vice president of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, spoke, saying that today

Joint Shipping by the Shipping Bureau and Longhai Railway Begins; Tonghua Ship Sails to Haizhou This Afternoon; Announcement to All Circles Yesterday and Stipulation of Freight Rates at Each Station; Longhai Railway Bureau Announces Process of Handling Joint Shipping

The state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (國營招商局) is about to formally sign a contract to undertake a national sea-land joint transportation agreement. It is scheduled to be fully implemented on the first day of next month. The Longhai Railway (隴海鐵路) has decided to implement it earlier, tomorrow, and will announce the truth about the joint transportation, as well as the methods and freight rates. The details are recorded as follows.

Goods Accumulated Awaiting Shipment

Over the past two days, Zhou Songnian (周頌年), the director of the Longhai Railway Bureau's Transportation Department, has repeatedly sent telegrams to Shanghai, stating that two large batches of joint transportation goods have arrived at the temporary pier at Lao Yao (老窰), one batch being 2,000 tons and the other being 1,000 tons, urgently awaiting loading for Shanghai. Upon receiving the report, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) urgently ordered the Tonghua (同華) ship to sail this afternoon to load the first batch of joint transportation goods to Shanghai and assigned the Yushun (遇順) ship to depart for Lao Yao on the 21st to rush the shipment of joint transportation goods to Shanghai. A reply telegram has been sent to Zhou Songnian for reference. The cargo line at the Jinliyuan (金利源) Wharf has also been prepared for the loading and unloading of incoming goods.

Implementing Joint Transportation

After the Longhai Railway and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) jointly manage sea-land transportation, they officially announced to all sectors of society yesterday: In order to seek benefits and convenience for agriculture and commerce, and reduce transportation costs, the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (國營招商局) and the state-owned Longhai Railway (國有隴海鐵路) will jointly manage sea-land transportation, so that goods from Shanghai, Qingdao, Xiamen, Guangzhou, and other coastal ports can directly reach Xuzhou, Lanfeng, Zhengzhou, Luoyang, Tongguan, and other places along the Longhai Railway. Agricultural products along the Longhai Railway can also be directly transported to the coastal ports. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) has assigned the Tonghua (同華) ship to sail from Shanghai to Lao Yao (老窰), Haizhou, at 12:00 noon today, arrive at Lao Yao on the 20th, load the first batch of joint transportation goods, and return to Shanghai from Lao Yao on the 22nd, arriving in Shanghai on the 24th. Kang Zhengji (康正記), who is undertaking the tugboat service at Lao Yao, has dispatched two barges, scheduled to be towed by the Tonghua to Lao Yao today.

Joint Transportation Methods

Joint transportation of goods from Shanghai to various stations along the Longhai Railway is divided into full-carload shipments and less-than-carload shipments. The joint transportation stations are Xinpu, A’hu Town, Xin’an Town, Yunhe, Xuzhou, Tongshan, Huangkou, Dangshan, Mamuji, Shangqiu, Liuhe, Minquan, Lanfeng, Kaifeng, Zhongmu, Zhengzhou, Sishui, Gongxian, Luodong, Huixing Town, Shanzhou, Changjiawan, Huandi Town, and Tongguan, totaling 24 stations. Procedures for joint transportation of goods from Shanghai to various stations along the Longhai Railway’s trunk and branch lines: (1) First, provide a list of goods, number of pieces, weight, or dimensions to the Sea-Land Joint Transportation Section of the Business Department of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商總局業務科水陸聯運股). (2) After the goods are loaded on the ship, take the customs declaration to the Business Department to exchange for a formal bill of lading. (3) After receiving the bill of lading, the cargo owner only needs to pick up the goods at the destination.

Full-Carload Freight Rates

Freight rates per metric ton for joint transportation of full-carload shipments from Shanghai to the following stations: Xinpu: first-class goods 9.75 yuan, second-class goods 8.18 yuan, third-class goods 7.70 yuan, fourth-class goods 5.31 yuan, fifth-class goods 5.10 yuan; Xuzhou: first-class goods 26.42 yuan, second-class goods 18.13 yuan, third-class goods 16.04 yuan, fourth-class goods 12.57 yuan, fifth-class goods 10.08 yuan; Shangqiu: first-class goods 36.82 yuan, second-class goods 33.20 yuan, third-class goods 20.33 yuan, fourth-class goods 16.85 yuan, fifth-class goods 12.69 yuan; Kaifeng: first-class goods 44.53 yuan, second-class goods 26.40 yuan, third-class goods 23.10 yuan, fourth-class goods 19.65 yuan, fifth-class goods 14.49 yuan; Zhengzhou: first-class goods 47.88 yuan, second-class goods 27.68 yuan, third-class goods 24.20 yuan, fourth-class goods 20.60 yuan, fifth-class goods 15.17 yuan; Luodong: first-class goods 53.47 yuan, second-class goods 29.73 yuan, third-class goods 25.88 yuan, fourth-class goods 21.92 yuan, fifth-class goods 16.18 yuan; Shanzhou: first-class goods 65.80 yuan, second-class goods 34.14 yuan, third-class goods 29.40 yuan, fourth-class goods 24.55 yuan, fifth-class goods 18.29 yuan; Tongguan: first-class goods 74.29 yuan, second-class goods 37.17 yuan, third-class goods 31.83 yuan, fourth-class goods 26.38 yuan, fifth-class goods 19.74 yuan.

Less-Than-Carload Shipments

Freight rates per 50 kilograms for joint transportation of less-than-carload shipments from Shanghai to the following stations: Xinpu: first-class goods 0.86 yuan, second-class goods 0.74 yuan, third-class goods 0.70 yuan, fourth-class goods 0.49 yuan, fifth-class goods 0.46 yuan; Xuzhou: first-class goods 1.95 yuan, second-class goods 1.38 yuan, third-class goods 1.24 yuan, fourth-class goods 0.95 yuan, fifth-class goods 0.79 yuan; Shangqiu: first-class goods 2.63 yuan, second-class goods 1.72 yuan, third-class goods 1.53 yuan, fourth-class goods 1.23 yuan, fifth-class goods 0.96 yuan; Kaifeng: first-class goods 3.12 yuan, second-class goods 1.91 yuan, third-class goods 1.70 yuan, fourth-class goods 1.41 yuan, fifth-class goods 1.07 yuan; Zhengzhou: first-class goods 3.33 yuan, second-class goods 2.00 yuan, third-class goods 1.77 yuan, fourth-class goods 1.47 yuan, fifth-class goods 1.12 yuan; Luodong: first-class goods 3.70 yuan, second-class goods 2.14 yuan, third-class goods 1.89 yuan, fourth-class goods 1.56 yuan, fifth-class goods 1.19 yuan; Shanzhou: first-class goods 4.51 yuan, second-class goods 2.43 yuan, third-class goods 2.11 yuan, fourth-class goods 1.74 yuan, fifth-class goods 1.33 yuan; Tongguan: first-class goods 5.06 yuan, second-class goods 2.62 yuan, third-class goods 2.26 yuan, fourth-class goods 1.85 yuan, fifth-class goods 1.43 yuan.

Announcement of the Process

Yesterday, the Longhai Railway Administration announced to the reporter of the New Sound News Agency the truth about the joint transportation between the Longhai Railway and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局): Since the Ministry of Railways advocated cooperation between various routes and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) to jointly manage sea-land transportation and signed a contract, the Longhai Railway, in order to respond to environmental needs and facilitate the circulation of agricultural products along the route, first formulated methods in accordance with the contract terms and scheduled implementation. However, private shipping companies, fearing that the cargo of the route would be monopolized by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局), rose up in opposition. These situations have all been reported in the newspapers, thus arousing the attention of the general public. This kind of event is a major improvement in the transportation industry and has a great impact on the future of commercial economy and agricultural products, and it should have research value. What is the current situation of the junction of the Longhai sea and land, and is the cargo transportation of private shipping companies really hopeless? It is difficult to understand the truth without detailed investigation. (1) The Longhai Railway is the largest east-west trunk line in the country, running through northern Jiangsu, central Henan, and reaching Xi'an, Shaanxi, via Tongguan. In terms of transportation position, it seems to be as important as the Yangtze River. The sea-land junction station at its eastern end is called Dapou (大浦), located on the bank of the Linhong River (臨洪河), with a pier built to berth ships traveling between Shanghai and Qingdao to load goods for sea transport. There are still more than 40 miles of waterway, and due to tidal conditions, navigation is not very smooth. This is a temporary pier of the route, and several private shipping companies are recruiting cargo. Whenever cargo is unobstructed and goods are prosperous, Dapou’s goods cannot be exported quickly, resulting in delays, which has long been a disease for merchants. Therefore, Dapou is one of the Longhai's export channels, but it cannot be the only export channel of the Longhai. The route had already foreseen this, so it tried its best to operate the Lianyungang (連雲海港) seaport to supplement the shortage of Dapou and the needs of cargo transportation. After the completion of Lianyungang seaport in the future, Dapou pier can still be a side branch for export. The rumor that Dapou pier will be abandoned is ignorant of the facts and is not credible. (2) Dapou pier cannot export goods smoothly, and the official pier of Lao Yao (老窰) in Lianyungang seaport has a huge project and cannot be completed immediately. If no other way is sought, there will be a risk of blockage and congestion of agricultural products in Shaanxi, Gansu, southern Shanxi, western Henan, and Xuhai, which will greatly affect the rural economy and people's livelihoods in the above-mentioned areas. The Longhai Railway Bureau is wary of the importance of this matter, so it is building a temporary pier and warehouses at Sunjiashan (孫家山), about ten miles west of Lao Yao, and is carrying out joint transportation methods with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商進行聯運辦法) in accordance with the Ministry's order, so that it can separate from Dapou's shipping and run in parallel. The rumor that the Longhai and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) are jointly managing sea-land transportation at the Lao Yao pier is also ignorant of the local situation. At present, the Lao Yao pier is still in the stage of driving piles and filling the sea, so how can it stop ships and manage joint transportation? Anyone with common sense knows that this is a rumor. (3) Currently, thousands of tons of goods have been piled up at the Dapou pier and cannot be transported smoothly. The more goods that come, the more congested Dapou becomes. The joint transportation between the Longhai and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) is therefore imminent due to this need and is now ready to be implemented soon. Some people say that after the Sunjiashan (孫家山) starts joint transportation, Dapou will be affected, and even those related to shipping there will inevitably suffer losses. This is also a wrong observation. It should be known that there has always been competition in the shipping industry, both in China and abroad. The start of sea-land joint transportation in Sunjiashan (孫家山) and Dapou's shipping will create competition, which is the actual situation. However, it is too much to say that Dapou will be greatly affected, because the Dapou station is still open to traffic as usual, and the Dapou pier is also loading and unloading as usual. As long as the shipping companies there improve their methods and try to solicit business, why worry about not having goods to transport? Although the Longhai cooperates with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) due to contractual relations, the transportation of goods is still subject to the opinions of merchants. If merchants insist on transporting to Dapou and handing over to private shipping companies for shipment, the Longhai cannot force them to hand over to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) for joint transportation. This is a clear principle. What is the loss? As for the current situation in Dapou, where there is too much cargo and it is difficult to ensure that the goods do not go to other routes, even without the competition from the temporary pier of Sunjiashan (孫家山), what is the benefit to Dapou? In short, the future of the Dapou pier depends on whether the shipping companies there have good methods. If they are well-managed and the water feet are low, even with joint transportation competition, there will be no impact.

The North China Sino-Japanese Negotiations Reported by the Japanese Side are Opposed and Suspended by the Legislative Yuan

According to the "China Press," (字林報) Japanese sources in this port state that Japanese Ambassador Arima (有吉) did not hold any negotiations with the Chinese authorities during his trip to Peiping, because if Arima had done so, China would have de facto recognized "Manchukuo". However, Huang Fu (黄郛) and Japanese Major General Okamura (岡村) did discuss unresolved Sino-Japanese issues under the guidance of the Japanese Ambassador, but they did so with special caution to ensure that the discussions did not go beyond the scope of the Tanggu Truce Agreement. Judging from the situation, it seems that Wang Jingwei's (汪精衛) agreement with the Japanese Ambassador to have Arima preside over political negotiations with the "Man" authorities was not implemented due to opposition from the Legislative Yuan. It is said that the two sides agreed on the following points: the general principles of transportation cooperation between China and the "Man" authorities; the "Man" authorities should set up a post office on the border, adjacent to the Chinese post office, and customs should follow this approach; the "Man" authorities should collect import and export duties on goods passing through customs; China should regard Manchuria as part of its territory and not collect export duties on goods entering Manchuria, but should collect taxes as if transporting goods from one province to another, and the same applies to import duties. The report concludes by saying that, according to Ota (大田) of the Japanese Embassy, China and the Japanese authorities (or Manchuria) will continue to discuss everything in detail, and important matters can be resolved through discussion. The so-called important matters probably refer to China's de facto recognition of "Manchukuo."

The Money Trade Pledges to Borrow One Million from the Ministry of Finance

According to Dagong News Agency (大公社), the Shanghai Money Trade Association (上海錢業公會) held an extraordinary general meeting of all members at its association's premises at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 16th). Over fifty representatives attended, with Qin Runqing (秦潤卿) presiding. He first reported that the Ministry of Finance (財部) intends to borrow 2.5 million in cash from the association, using 5 million in 22nd-year customs treasury bills as collateral. After discussion among the representatives of the members, it was agreed that due to the current period of commercial depression, the money trade itself often shows signs of exhaustion. The Ministry of Finance had borrowed money not long ago, and now, before it has recovered its breath, it is even more powerless. However, the suppression of the Red Army is as urgent as fire and cannot be delayed. In order to do the best of the money trade, it was unanimously decided to pledge one million yuan. The method is that each large and small remittance bank will be assigned 10,000 yuan. There are a total of 65 banks in the city, totaling 650,000 yuan. The remaining 350,000 yuan will be subsidized by the Money Trade Reserve. It is said that the Money Trade Association notified each bank yesterday to pay the full amount within three days.

The Ministry of Railways Orders Correction of the Temporary Regulations for Joint Transportation of Responsible Goods

Yesterday, the Two-Route Administration (兩路管理局) received an instruction from the Ministry of Railways (鐵道部) with the number Lian Zi 7294 (聯字第七二九四號), stating that after investigating the temporary regulations for joint transportation of responsible goods by the railway, which had been issued for compliance, it was found that there were slight errors in the typesetting of the articles within the regulations, which should be corrected as follows: Article 33: Each joint transportation route shall use its own open wagons as flatcars (hereinafter referred to as factory cars) to transport joint transportation goods. When tarpaulins and ropes are required, the tarpaulins and ropes of the route must be used and transported directly with the car. The rent for these tarpaulins and ropes will not be calculated separately. All tarpaulins covering joint transportation wagons shall be covered in accordance with the provisions of Article 72 of the detailed rules for responsible transportation of wagons. The front end of the front sheet should cover the front end of the rear sheet to prevent the intrusion of wind, rain, and fire embers. If this car changes direction after passing the track, the starting station should calculate the mileage traveled by the car so that the longest route of the vehicle can be covered in the forward direction. If it travels in the opposite direction on this route or another route, and it is considered that the seams of the tarpaulin are easily invaded by wind, rain, and fire embers, the route may add another tarpaulin to the original car. However, this added tarpaulin should be removed by the route when it is handed over to another route and should not be transported directly. Article 34: The acceptance of tarpaulins and ropes for joint transportation of direct open wagons shall be integrated with the acceptance of the vehicle as a whole. The method is to record the route number of the tarpaulin and rope in the vehicle, the delivery notice, and the route sheet, and accept them together. In addition to separate orders, the above two corrected articles are combined and ordered to be complied with. After receiving the order, the bureau has transferred it to the Transportation Department for compliance. (New News Agency)
