The Dancer Yin Qiulian is Indeed Chinese; Judge Liu Solemnly Declared Yesterday; The Case Has Been Heard and the Verdict Will Be Announced on the 20th

The dancer Yin Qiulian (尹秋蓮) sued her companion Gao Lili (高利利) for injury. When the First Special District Court (第一特區地方法院) opened the trial a few days ago, Yin spoke English and claimed to be from "Manchukuo." After the news was published in the newspapers, society paid more attention to it. The trial judge, Liu Yugui (劉毓桂), also believed that the issue of Yin's nationality needed to be re-examined. The original plan to announce the verdict yesterday afternoon was therefore suspended, and both sides were specially summoned for oral arguments. At around 3:00 PM, Judge Liu opened the court and announced the reasons for reopening the debate, saying (1) that the case was not fully understood and (2) that the plaintiff's nationality needed to be investigated. He then asked Yin Qiulian about her address and place of origin. Yin still made her statement in English, which was translated into Chinese by an interpreter. She said that she lived at No. 160 Bazilu (靶子路), that her family was originally from Shenyang, and that her parents had always been in Shenyang, where she also grew up. However, because she had received Japanese education, she did not know Mandarin. Although she understood a little, she could not speak it. The defendant's defense lawyer, Chao Kun (巢堃), immediately stood up and stated that the lawyer had gone to Anle Palace (安樂宮) for field investigation and learned that the plaintiff could not only speak Mandarin but also Shanghai dialect. According to her employer, Lu Zuting (陸祖庭), manager Chen (陳姓), and supervisor Yang Mao Yuan (楊毛媛), Yin used a northern accent when talking to them on weekdays. Now that she says she cannot speak Mandarin, it is intentional deception. However, since she said she understood a little, why didn't she immediately state that she was not a "Manchukuo person" when the interpreter translated the word "Manchukuo person" last time? Moreover, the plaintiff's lawyer is good at English. If the interpreter had mistranslated, he should have objected, but he did not correct it. As for Frank, who testified in court last time, claiming to be the manager of the dance hall, was also false. The foreign manager of the dance hall is named Mass. This one spot can reveal the rest, and it can be seen that the plaintiff is all false. The plaintiff's lawyer, Jiang Zongpan (江宗泮), identified it as an interpreter's mistranslation, saying that because of this one sentence, it has aroused social attention. Not only are Chinese newspapers reporting it, but also Japanese newspapers. However, the plaintiff only said she was Manchurian, and the defendant's lawyer immediately dragged her into being a "Manchukuo person," which should not have this view. Judge Liu then declared that this issue was not within the scope of the case, because the plaintiff stated in the complaint that her place of origin was Fengtian, and that day the plaintiff answered the question of her place of origin in English as "Mukden." He heard it very clearly. However, he did not know why it was translated into the word "Manchukuo." Now that the plaintiff has stated that her place of origin is Shenyang, the three eastern provinces are our country's territory, and the people of the three eastern provinces are of course the people of the Republic of China. The plaintiff's expression of intention is very clear, so he hopes that both parties will not discuss the issue of nationality. Judge Liu then repeatedly questioned the plaintiff about the accusations and had the lawyers on both sides re-debate the case, and then ordered the verdict to be announced on the 20th of this month. Furthermore, according to a letter from lawyers Song Chunfang (宋春舫) and Jiang Zongpan (江宗泮), "We, the undersigned, according to the statement of the client Yin Qiulian, yesterday, the newspapers reported a piece of news about the dancer Yin Qiulian suing Gao Lili for the crime of injury. Because the facts are not in accordance with the facts, we have been entrusted to correct it in the record. At the re-opening of the debate today, with regard to the point of nationality, the presiding judge declared in court, 'During the last court hearing, Yin Qiulian did reply with the word (Mukden), that is, Feng (tian or Shenyang), and her complaint also stated the place of origin of Fengtian. Today, she also replied that she is a Chinese person from Fengtian. ' Because the facts have been clarified, this matter is related to the national system and is not shallow, so we ask you to correct it again," According to this corresponding letter, I hope you will check the correction, and to the Shenbao Museum, lawyers Song Chunfang and Jiang Zongpan, November 18th."

The Monk Kaijue Has Been Imprisoned for More Than a Year; Yesterday, He Was Able to See the Light of Day Again; Kaijue Describes the Process of Being Sent to the Tramp Institute by Kaisheng; He Was Abused and Forbidden to See Guests; He Asked the Judge to Extend Justice; || The Result Was That Both Monks Were Released on Bail and the Hearing Was Rescheduled ||

The abbot monk Kaisheng (開生) of Guoren Temple (國恩寺) on Villemont Road in the French Concession of this port and the abbot monk Kaijue (開覺) of Chaoyin Cave (潮音洞) on Putuo Mountain (普陀山) are half-brothers from the same master. Both temples are subordinate to the Zizhulin (紫竹林) branch temple on Putuo Mountain. Because the two monks were competing for the current abbot's position, Kaisheng, taking advantage of Kaijue's opportunity to come to Shanghai last year to collect vow money, reported to Wang Yiting (王一亭), a standing committee member of the Buddhist Association, and sent a letter to the Shanghai South Longhua Vagrant Training Institute (滬南龍華游民習勤所) to imprison Kaijue on the grounds that he did not abide by the rules of the temple. He was forbidden to communicate with or meet with people. Until recently, Kaijue's younger brother, also his cousin Jingan (淨安), came to Shanghai and learned about it. He hired a lawyer and went to visit him to inquire about the reasons for his imprisonment. He hired lawyer Li Mian (黎冕) to file a criminal self-accusation with the Second Special District Court (第二特區地方法院), accusing

Kaisheng of Obstructing Freedom

And an incidental civil suit for damages. According to the complaint, on the 31st of last month, Judge Li Changnian (李昌年) opened the court to summon and question him, but because the plaintiff was imprisoned and the defendant Kaisheng claimed to be ill and did not arrive, he was instructed to reschedule the hearing. The details have been recorded in the previous newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, the date for the continued hearing arrived again. The court prepared a document and sent bailiffs to the Vagrant Training Institute to bring the plaintiff Kaijue to court. The two lawyers he hired, Li Mian (黎冕) and Dong Banggan (董邦幹), also arrived on time. The defendant Kaisheng also arrived at the court with his defense lawyers, Li Fengshen (李逢申) and Tu Zhengou (屠振鵠), to wait for the hearing. There were many friends and fellow monks related to both parties who came to court to observe, causing the Second Court

Unusual Crowding

There was no room to insert a foot. Those who arrived later had to stand outside the court, craning their necks to watch. At 2:30, Judge Li and the clerk Wang Baoxun (王葆薰) took their seats, called the parties and lawyers on both sides to the court, and first questioned the defendant Kaisheng about the process of imprisoning Kaijue in the Vagrant Training Institute. According to his answer, he and Kaijue were brothers from the same master. Because he did not abide by the rules of the temple, he often came to pester him, opened a smoking den on the upper floor of Yongtai Tobacco and Paper Store (永泰烟紙店) at No. 90 Huanghe Road (黄河路), and ordered a 10 yuan vegetarian meal at Juelin Vegetarian Restaurant (覺林素菜館) for no reason, and invited guests to Guoren Temple (國恩寺), but did not pay for the meal, and stole clothes worth dozens of yuan. Because of his various unruly behaviors, he reported to

Buddhist Layman Wang Yiting

And wrote a letter to send him to the Vagrant Training Institute to make him change his ways. He was completely well-intentioned, so he paid six yuan for his meals every month. If he was malicious, why would he be willing to pay for his meals? He was asked how Kaijue often came to pester him. He answered that he often came to borrow money from him to spend and did not pay it back. Last year, he borrowed 150 yuan twice, first borrowing 100 yuan in mid-June and then borrowing 50 yuan in mid-September. The abbot monk of Sanguantang (三官堂) on Putuo Mountain (普陀山) wrote a note as proof. When providing the note, he presented a note (written on octavo letter paper) to the court. After examining the note, the official asked, "If you borrowed money from you in June and September of last year, why does the note say March of the 22nd year?" Kaisheng hesitated and replied that it was

Abbot Monk of Sanguantang

Who wrote it and he didn't know. The official asked, "Do you know how to read?" He replied that he did not know how to read. Then he laughed and replied that he knew a few words. The official then gave the note to Kaisheng to read. After Kaisheng took the note and looked at it, he said, "This is the 23rd year. This note was written last year." Then he changed his mind and said, "This is the 22nd year. I remembered it wrong. I didn't write the note." The official asked again, "Can your temple regulations be handled like this?" He replied, "According to the temple regulations, if they don't obey the command of the residents and don't abide by the rules of the temple, they can be handled even if they are elders." At this point, the official ordered the plaintiff Kaijue to be brought to the court. According to his statement, he and Kaisheng were master brothers of the same generation, and he called his master uncle. Their relationship has always been ordinary. He was asked, "Have you ever borrowed money from Kaisheng and written a note?" He replied, "I have never borrowed money from him or written a note. My own temple is Chaoyin Cave (潮音洞), which has an income of 10,000 yuan in incense money a year. Guoren Temple (國恩寺) has an income of 30,000 yuan. It's all his [Kaisheng's]".

Damaging My Reputation

I was the caretaker of the Chao Yin Cave on Mount Putuo since the twelfth year of the Republic [1923]. Since my master passed away last year, he has been bullying me and dealing with me in this way. His lawyer presented eight account books dating back to the thirteenth year of the Republic [1924] regarding the Chao Yin Cave when I was the caretaker. I am asked how I was confined in the vagrant labor camp. I answered that I was the caretaker of the Chao Yin Cave on Mount Putuo. Because the temple is near the sea, the hall was damaged by a typhoon the year before last. Last year, a pilgrim came to the mountain to burn incense and promised to contribute money for repairs. Because the money had not been fully collected, I came to Shanghai to collect the promised donations. Later, I developed heart and stomach pains and was hospitalized for treatment. Kaisheng sent Shen Yuanlin to the hospital to call me and said that his grand-disciple Yuanlin was smoking opium and violating the rules.

Calling Me to Accompany Him to Be Sent Away

He wanted me to accompany him to the vagrant labor camp for opium cessation. I thought it was a good deed to send someone to quit opium, so I agreed to go to Guogen Temple on October 21st. Kaisheng told me to hire a car to send Yuanlin to the vagrant labor camp. Unexpectedly, upon arrival, I was immediately detained and not allowed to return. They said all sorts of bad things about me, stripped me of my clothes, made me wear vagrant clothes, and locked me in a dark prison. I had no tea or water to drink all day, and the food was not enough to eat. I was also handcuffed and not allowed to speak. If I disobeyed, I would be hit on the palm of my hand two or three hundred times, I do not know the exact number. I was beaten several times and not allowed visitors until after this lawyer came to see me, when I was moved to another room with slightly better treatment. Now my

Whole Body Aches

I also have a lump in my chest. I request an examination. I also stated that Guogen Temple and Chao Yin Cave are both subordinate temples of the Zizhu Forest. The abbots of the two temples are supposed to rotate every three years. Kaisheng's term was up, and he should have been rotated to become the abbot of Guogen Temple. He did this to me because he was afraid that I would take his position as abbot, declaring that he would imprison me until I die, so that he could do whatever he wanted afterwards. Since I was imprisoned, all the affairs of the Chao Yin Cave have been taken over by Kaisheng. Also, because Guang Sheng was very harsh to the visiting monks in Guogen Temple, and the visiting monks told me about it, I advised Kaisheng about it. Because of this, he hated and envied me, and took

Such Cruel and Vicious Measures

to imprison me. Now I do not want to go back to the vagrant labor camp. I would rather face a lawsuit here. I ask for justice. If the judge finds any illegal behavior on my part, he can punish me severely. I will gladly accept it. The judge then asked if anyone from the Buddhist Association was present. At this point, Yuan Xilian, the lawyer who had been commissioned by the defendant to appear in court, withdrew from representing the defendant yesterday and appeared on behalf of the Buddhist Association, stating, "Our lawyer is the perennial legal advisor of the Buddhist Association. Today, I am here on behalf of the Buddhist Association to state that the Buddhist Association received a report from Kaisheng about Kaijue's various illegal activities, which were investigated and resolved. A letter was sent to the vagrant labor camp. If the court needs to ask about the detailed circumstances at that time,"

Representative of the Buddhist Association

"Is also present in court today and can be summoned for questioning." The judge then summoned him. According to Wang Junhe, who filed the case, he works in the secretariat of the Buddhist Association. He said that he was present in court today to observe the proceedings. The personnel who handled this matter before have left their positions, and he does not know the details. He said that he would need to ask layman Wang Yiting and could reply in writing later. Wang then left. The defendant then claimed, "My appointment as caretaker of the Chao Yin Cave was at the request of the people, not a seizure of his position." At this point, the judge said that the case still needed to be investigated and that the defendant's statement of defense had not yet been filed. He then asked the lawyers from both sides if they had any opinions. The lawyers from both sides

Expressed Their Opinions on the Case

and argued fiercely. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that the plaintiff had been illegally detained for more than a year and that the court should release him today and restore his freedom. As a result, the court ordered both parties to post bail and await another hearing at a later date. The defendant was also ordered to submit a statement of defense within three days. Because yesterday was Saturday and it was late when court adjourned, filing a statement and posting bail would have been impossible. The lawyers from both sides requested that they be temporarily responsible for the bail. Both parties left and would submit formal bail bonds on Monday. The court granted permission and ordered the lawyers from both sides to issue letters of guarantee for filing. Both parties left with their respective lawyers. The plaintiff, Kaijue, had been imprisoned for a year and a month and was only able to regain his freedom yesterday. However, it is still difficult to predict who will win in the future.

County Agricultural Education Center Holds the Fifth Annual Plowing Competition - 317 Heads of Cattle Participating, No. 1 and Five Others Performed Best

The Fifth Annual Plowing Competition organized by the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center was held at Zhuanqiao on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road. A goat and sheep exhibition was also held at the same time. Details are as follows:

A Glimpse of the Venue

The venue for the conference was located at Zhuanqiao Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road. A large archway was set up on Zhongshan Road, with a colorful banner on top that read "Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center Fifth Plowing Competition". The lecture hall was filled with chrysanthemums, and hundreds of prizes from all walks of life were displayed on the platform, dazzling the eyes. The cattle field was located at "Daidan Field", and the goat and sheep exhibition fields were located on both sides of Jianshe Road. There were four registration points set up in the field. The cattle participating in the competition were classified and arranged according to their age.

Participating Cattle

At 5 a.m. that morning, the center's bell rang to announce the start of the day, and all staff gathered in front of the lecture hall at 6 a.m. After the president reported on the division of duties, they set off to various teahouses to publicize the event. Farmers participated enthusiastically, with a total of 317 heads of cattle competing. There were even more goats and sheep, including a Holstein and a Swiss calf, which were particularly distinctive. They were displayed in the field for everyone to see.

Participating Representatives

Representatives attending the meeting included Cai Wuji of the Ministry of Industry, Huang Meixian of the Construction Department, Chen Shaohui of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, Pan Zhongjia of the Fifth Administrative Supervisory Office, Wu Huanru of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Director Wang of the Municipal Health Bureau, Zhang Jingye and Chen Jiapu of the County Party Department, Shi She, Zhu Yingge, Zheng Guozhai, and Yang Huiming of the County Education Bureau, Fan Ruichi of the Provincial People's Education Center, Gu Shaochang of the Jiading Agricultural Extension Institute, Qin Huang of the Xianyi School, and the Xin'an Children's Touring Group, totaling more than 500 people. The center's National Goods Exhibition Room and Agricultural Products Exhibition Room were specially opened for the day.

Opening Ceremony

The opening ceremony was held at 9 a.m. The chairman was Zhang Yi, the master of ceremonies was Ma Congdao, and the recorder was Chen Jiapu. First, honorary president Pan Zhongjia performed the unveiling ceremony, followed by the chairman's opening speech. Then, Chen Shaohui of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, Huang Meixian of the Jiangsu Construction Department, County Governor Pan Zhongjia, and Qian Zhongnan of the Social Affairs Bureau delivered speeches. Finally, Yang Yongxing of the Xin'an Children's Touring Group, Shen Jiucheng of the Shengsheng Livestock Farm, and Director Shi She of the County Education Bureau gave speeches in succession. The ceremony concluded with loud slogans.

Slogans

(1) Plowing cattle work hard and contribute greatly; (2) Plowing cattle are loyal and honest; (3) Everyone should protect the health of plowing cattle; (4) Everyone should study the raising of plowing cattle; (5) Healthy plowing cattle can increase farming efficiency; (6) Healthy plowing cattle can increase production volume; (7) Plowing competition is a national salvation effort; (8) Plowing competition is a rural salvation effort.

Cattle Parade

In the afternoon, there was a cattle parade. Flowers were added to the heads of the cattle and sheep, and gongs were sounded to lead the way. Slogans were shouted loudly. Wherever the cattle went, the road was blocked by onlookers. Members brought plowing cattle, goats, and sheep to the meeting, registered in advance, and then were given participation certificates. They were led to the cattle field or exhibition field according to their category. At the same time, they were given two coupons, one for food and one for a plow. Each member was given a plow. The participating farmers were all overjoyed.

Judging Meeting

Following the parade, there was a judging meeting, chaired by Cai Wuji. The judging criteria and scoring methods were approved, and judging duties were assigned. The judging then began. As a result, cattle numbered 1, 2, 23, 61, and 21 were judged to have performed the best. All prizes will be distributed by the prize-giving committee on the 21st of this month.

The Shanghai Real Estate Association has repeatedly received comparative tables of new and old water bills from its members Deli Company and Gu Lanji, requesting that it negotiate with the Municipal Council to promptly order the water company to turn on the water and convene a water fee committee. The association has sent two letters to the Municipal Council, requesting that it protect the lives of tax-paying citizens. The relevant documents are excerpted as follows:

Water Bill Comparison: "Deli Company" is located in Baishou Lane between Pingliang Road, Huasheng Road, and Fenzhou Road. Under the contracted water system, the total cost for six months was 1,083 yuan and 40 cents. Now, under the water meter system, the cost for six months is 2,187 yuan, 27 cents, more than double the previous amount. Baifu, Bailu, and Lane, located between Huasheng Road, Yangzhou Road, and Fenzhou Road, cost 1,347 yuan and 09 cents for six months under the contracted water system. Now, under the water meter system, the cost for six months is 3,017 yuan, 65 cents, an increase of one and a half times compared to the previous amount. "Gu Lanji" is located on Yuanfang Road, Zhoujiazui Road, Hongkou. Under the contracted water system, the cost for six months was 39 yuan and 12 cents. As for the water fee issue, we will wait for the committee to convene and discuss the matter at length. (2) Sirs, we are writing to inform you that we have received a letter from the Deli Management Accounting Office, a member of our association, stating that we are now sending two copies of a list of the old and new water fee price ratios for Baifu Lane, Bailu Lane, and Baishou Lane, located between Pingliang Road and Yangzhou Road, so that you can understand the true situation. Respectfully, [addressed to] General Manager Zhong of the Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council.

Moving Stones and Selling Strips, Kidnappers Set Up Traps to Separate Families, Two Cases Solved Together, Criminals Handed Over to the Public Security Bureau

Zhang Wang, a woman from Changzhou, is 37 years old. Her husband, Zhang Heshang, suddenly went blind six years ago and has not recovered his sight. As a result, they have been living off their savings, and their livelihood has been cut off. On the 12th of this month, she brought her seven-year-old daughter, Rongguan, to Shanghai, intending to work in a cloth factory. She had a relative living at No. 8 Hengqing Lane on Baylor Road. When she first arrived in Shanghai, after getting off at the Xieqiao stop, she asked a police officer for directions. Suddenly, a man lightly patted her shoulder and said that he could take her there. She was very grateful and followed him. The man then asked her about her life and learned that she had come to work. He then said that he could not recommend her to work in Shanghai without a guarantor. He had a friend who was a factory foreman and would do a good deed by introducing her. The woman thought that they had met by chance and that she had found a good friend, so she thanked him and went with him. When they arrived at the teahouse, the man said that she was covered in dust and should wash her face and drink tea while waiting for his friend to come. The woman then washed her face, and while her face was bent over the washbasin, the man carried her daughter away. After the woman finished washing, she looked around for her daughter and the so-called good man, but they were nowhere to be found. She shouted, but no one responded. She knew that she had been tricked and cried loudly, but there was nothing she could do. As a result, the woman looked for her daughter every day for eight days, pawning almost everything she had. Until the day before yesterday, she saw the man who had kidnapped her child in a hotel in Baoyu Lane, Caishi Street, drinking quietly. She immediately went inside and grabbed him, saying, "Let's go back to Xieqiao to discuss it." They went together to a teahouse in Xieqiao, and some hooligans were called out. They said to the woman, "The person is gone, but we can give you dozens of yuan to settle the matter." The woman refused and grabbed his chest. The man then became violent and escaped. The woman shouted "Catch the kidnapper!" Just then, Liu Yigao, a rickshaw puller, whose six-year-old son, Xiaolong, had also been kidnapped eight days earlier, was investigating the kidnappers. Upon hearing that a kidnapper had been caught, he realized that it was his enemy. He immediately chased after him, grabbed him, and called the police to take him to the Second District Police Station. It was learned that his name was Jin Ming and that he specialized in kidnapping. The woman's daughter and Liu's son were both kidnapped by the same gang, which had set up traps. Kidnapping boys was called "moving stones," and kidnapping girls was called "selling strips." Because two cases had been solved together, the man was immediately sent to the Public Security Bureau, and he was transferred to the local court for interrogation yesterday.

If we are truly grateful for your thorough prohibition, we will be deeply grateful. Respectfully, [addressed to] Police Chief of the Public Concession Municipal Council.

Recent Construction Status of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee

The Engineering and Reconstruction Group of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee yesterday released an overview of the projects in various districts. "District 1" (including Kaocheng Simingtang, Lanfeng Tongwaxiang, and Wenxian in Henan): The embankment line in Kaocheng has been repeatedly surveyed and estimated, and it has been slightly changed compared to the old embankment foundation. A total of 47,135 cubic meters of earthwork is estimated, requiring 9,570.04 yuan, including the cost of the construction site. Construction started on October 10. There are now more than 2,000 flood workers, and more than half of the work has been completed. It is expected to be completed by the end of the year. The breach filling in Lanfeng also started on October 10. 32,000 burlap sacks have been thrown in. There are now more than 2,000 flood workers every day, and the earthwork has risen above the water surface. There is still seven-tenths of the work remaining, and it is also expected to be completed by the end of the year. There are a total of 19 large and small sluice gates in Wenxian, all of which have been surveyed and estimated. It is scheduled to start construction before the 11th of this month and is expected to be completed by the end of the year. The above are all earthworks. As for the stone dams that should be built, they are still being surveyed and estimated. "District 2" (North Bank of Changyuan, Hebei): There are the most breaches on the north bank of Changyuan. There are a total of 30 breaches, large and small, within 20 kilometers from Shitou Village Railway Station. The 29th breach has now been blocked. The 1st to 26th breaches are all dry breaches, which have been divided into ten sections for contract construction. Construction started at the end of October and is scheduled to be completed by the end of this month. The 27th and 30th breaches are the most severe and have caused the most damage. The water flow has not stopped until now, and the project is more difficult. Currently, resources and manpower are concentrated here in order to block the water before the freezing period. According to reports, the first, second, and fourth channels of the water inlet have been significantly silted up after being hung with willow trees. The situation is very good. However, the water flow is concentrated, and the third channel is flowing very rapidly. A diversion canal is being excavated outside the water inlet, and a water-facing dam is being built to divert the water from the water inlet back to the river channel. 300 American pine trees and tens of thousands of burlap sacks have been purchased and transported, along with more than 60 tons of lead, which will be transported twice via the Pinghan Railway. Other materials are also being purchased and transported in order to carry out large-scale damming, which will be successful in the near future. "District 3" (Xiaopang Village on the south bank of Changyuan, Hebei): After correcting the embankment line for damming the breach, the earthwork is calculated to be 72,774.94 cubic meters, which is divided into seven sections for contract construction. Construction started on October 26 and is scheduled to be completed within 41 days. Later, the height of the embankment was increased by five centimeters, increasing the earthwork by more than 6,000 cubic meters, for a total of 79,133.37 cubic meters, estimated to require 48,208.17 yuan. There are 3,000 flood workers currently, and one-quarter of the work has been completed. It is expected to be completed by the end of the year.

Liu Xiang Asks for Strict Prohibition of Tax Evasion on Postal Parcels of Cigarettes, Sends Letter to Postal Administration to Issue Circular for Prohibition

According to the Xinxin News Agency, the 21st Army of Sichuan Province's anti-communist campaign has already issued an order for a general offensive and has achieved great victories. However, tax revenue is short, which is detrimental to military needs. Recently, various tax bureaus in Sichuan Province have submitted reports, stating that merchants in Shanghai, Hankou, Yichang, and other places are packing cigarettes into small boxes, forming postal parcels, without any factory tax receipts, and sending them through the post office to various counties in Sichuan Province, hoping to evade Chongqing-Wan County taxes and duties, which affects military needs. The headquarters of the 21st Army has now informed the Eastern Sichuan Postal Administration, which forwarded a letter to the Shanghai Postal Administration, ordering all provinces to investigate and prohibit it. Postal parcels sent from the Shanghai Postal Administration must be inspected by customs. Various cigarettes cannot be sent without factory tax receipts. However, postal branches in Hankou, Yichang, and Minhang and Zhoujiaqiao near Shanghai can send parcels without tax receipts. There must be some tax evasion, which affects not only the cigarette tax revenue of Sichuan Province. The postal authorities should order all bureaus to prohibit the sending of parcels without tax receipts in accordance with regulations.

Fu Hua Goes to Digang to Rescue the Stranded Qingpu Steamer - The Forecastle of the Qingpu Takes on Water and Collides with the Digang Wharf

The Qingpu steamer of the Sanbei Company ran aground in Digang and damaged the Digang wharf. The situation is quite serious. The details are as follows:

Damage to the Wharf: It is found that the Qingpu steamer ran aground in front of the Hanyeping wharf in Digang. At the time of the accident, it somehow sailed into the Hanyeping wharf and ran aground on the shallow shore. At that time, when the ship moved sideways into the wharf, it collided with the wharf due to its heavy load. The outer barrier of the wharf was damaged. A ship of the Japanese Postal Coastal Society carrying iron ore sand was docked outside the wharf, but fortunately it was not hit. As for the extent of the damage to the wharf, Shanghai is not yet able to know in detail.

Damage to the Forecastle: The shallow beach where the Qingpu was stranded is not sandy, but a rocky beach. Therefore, the heavy-laden Qingpu collided heavily when it suddenly rushed in. It is heard that the bottom of the Qingpu's forecastle has been broken and is taking on water. The company has not publicly announced the details of the accident and the damage, so it is only known that the ship has been broken, and the situation is quite serious, but the detailed situation is not yet known.

Fu Hua to the Rescue: The ship cannot be rescued at present. Yesterday, the company decided to send the newly renovated upstream river steamer Fu Hua to tow a large iron barge and depart from Shanghai this morning to Digang to unload the cargo and passengers from the Qingpu to Shanghai, and then try to tow the Qingpu out of danger. The loss of the damaged wharf will be investigated and verified separately. Therefore, there is no hope of rescuing the Qingpu in the short term.

Protracted Three Friends Lawsuit Remains Unresolved, Special First District Court Assists in Execution

The labor-capital dispute case of the Three Friends Industrial Company in Pudong has been in court for nearly two years since the capital side refused to accept the arbitration decision of the Municipal Government. In April of this year, the Supreme Court ruled to reject the capital side's appeal and handed it over to the Shanghai District Court for execution according to law. Although the court repeatedly ordered both parties to go out and find ways to reconcile, the capital side had no sincerity, so the two parties could not approach each other. On the 24th of last month, when the court opened the twelfth execution hearing, it determined that reconciliation had failed and, because the capital side's head office was located in the Public Concession, decided to entrust the First Special District Court to assist in the execution of the dismissal fee of 75,095 yuan for the dismissed employees. After receiving the letter, the First Special District Court opened a hearing at 9:00 AM on the 17th of this month. Zhang Yihai and Gong Yuting, representatives of the camp, and lawyer Wei Wenhan, the agent, and Zhang Shizhao, the agent lawyer of the capital side, were present. Judge Jiang ascended the twelfth court for questioning and ordered the capital side's agent lawyer to convey to the company to pay the full amount of the dismissal fee within ten days, otherwise, the company would be sealed up. Then he announced the adjournment.

Anglo-American Tobacco Factory Workers Petitioned Yesterday - Yu Hongjun Agreed to Order the Factory to Revise Factory Regulations, but Advised Workers Not to Take Excessive Actions

Xin Sheng She reports that the Anglo-American Tobacco Company has repeatedly refused to revise the labor-capital treaty and does not allow the union to collect membership fees. All workers are brewing a strike. The union petitioned the party and government organs yesterday. The details are as follows:

Refusal to Revise Conditions

The contract revised in the sixteenth year between the Anglo-American Tobacco Company's labor and capital is inconsistent with the current treatment. More than 3,600 workers requested the union to propose revisions. The union submitted a request to the Social Affairs Bureau in the spring of this year to revise it. Because of the re-election of the union at that time, a dispute occurred, so the Social Affairs Bureau issued an order to suspend the progress. After the re-election was completed, the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union repeatedly urged the authorities to expedite the handling. The Social Affairs Bureau summoned and mediated several times, but the company submitted a written report, saying that the current Factory Law no longer requires the existence of a labor-capital contract, so it repeatedly refused to attend, making it impossible to proceed.

No Collection of Membership Fees Allowed

Since the capital side repeatedly refused to negotiate and revise the labor-capital contract, the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union held a representative meeting in November to discuss the revision of the treaty and asked the Municipal Government for arbitration. On the 16th of this month, the union went to the gate of the new and old factories as usual to collect membership fees when the workers were off work. Unexpectedly, the factory strictly refused and even sounded the police to drive them away. The company usually lets female workers off work at about 2:00 PM, and male workers at 5:00 PM. On that day, it notified the staff of each workshop in advance to inform the workers not to pay membership fees, and ordered male and female workers to leave the factory at the same time when they were off work. Thousands of workers poured out, making it impossible for the union to collect fees.

Union Petitions Party and Government

The Fifth District Cigarette Industry Union believes that the capital side's actions are deliberately undermining the labor movement. Yesterday morning, it sent representatives Chen Peide, Lou Jingguan, Li Chunde, Hong Meiquan, Yin Shigeng, Chen Shaoqing, and others to petition the party and government organs, requesting the speedy revision of the conditions. First, they went to the Municipal Party Department, where Zhou Lianze, the director of the Civil Training Section, received them. He promised to submit the workers' request to the Municipal Government and expedite the revision, and ordered the factory to accept mediation. Yu Hongjun, the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, received them and promised to approve the revision of the factory regulations and continue to negotiate the conditions in the near future. He also promised to correct the factory's actions and advised the representatives not to take excessive actions and wait for the party and government to mediate. When they arrived at the Social Affairs Bureau, because yesterday was Saturday, the office hours had passed, so the representatives left a petition and returned.

Last night, Mr. Xi Guansheng, the general manager of the company, specially initiated a chrysanthemum appreciation party on the third floor of the restaurant, inviting celebrities from all walks of life. More than 100 guests attended, including Wang Yiting, Wen Hongen, Yan Duhe, Zhang Zhuping, Li Dachao, Zheng Zhengqiu, etc. They were all talents of the times. After a few rounds of wine, Mr. Xi stood up and delivered a welcome speech, stating the performances of enjoying chrysanthemums together, promoting horticulture, and farmer-worker cooperation. Next were speeches by Yan Duhe, Zheng Zhengqiu, Qian Shou Tie, Cui Tongyue, and other gentlemen. At the end was the vocal performance of Hong Songjiong, a member of the Shanghai Flower and Tree Association, to add to the fun. It was not until 10:30 PM that everyone dispersed in high spirits. It is heard that the chrysanthemum competition will be judged tonight, and the results of the evaluation will be announced tomorrow.

Fang Jiufu Silver Shop in Nanshi Robbed

At 5:30 PM the day before yesterday, Fang Jiufu Silver Shop, a newly opened shop with house number 4 at the intersection of Malu Bridge on Nanshi Station Road, was suddenly visited by two robbers, one wearing a grey cloth cotton robe and the other wearing blue cloth shirt and pants. Both spoke with a Jiangbei accent. When the two approached the counter, the robber in the robe immediately asked to buy something, while the robber in short attire immediately pulled out a pistol, forbidding the shop assistants from making a sound. At the same time, the robber in the robe jumped into the counter and robbed six gold rings, five pairs of gold earrings, three pairs of screw earrings, three gilded bracelets, three gilded hairpins, two gilded rings, and seven gold circles, weighing about sixteen taels in total. After obtaining the loot, they fled westward. Afterwards, the shop owner filed a report with the Huining Road Police Station of the Second District General Office, which was forwarded to the General Bureau's Inspection Office and Detective Team to pay attention to arresting the robbers.

Jiangsu Province Exempts Tuition and Accommodation Fees for All Provincial Middle Schools, Effective in the Second Semester of This Year

The tuition and accommodation fees collected by all provincial middle schools in Jiangsu Province amount to 200,000 yuan annually. This amount is listed in the Jiangsu Provincial Education Budget as administrative income to be formally disbursed as regular expenses. After the Jiangsu Provincial Government approved the exemption of tuition and accommodation fees for all provincial middle schools, the "school administrative income" item in the education budget was reduced by 200,000 yuan. The method of offsetting this is to add two jiao per shi (unit of dry measure) under the Caomi (tribute rice) provincial tax item. The total tribute rice levy in Jiangsu Province is approximately 1.5 million shi per year. Due to harvest failures and arrears from the people, it is not possible to collect the full amount. After discounts, the amount will be about 200,000 yuan, calculated at two jiao per shi, which will be used to offset the exemption of tuition and accommodation fees. It is understood that the tribute rice tax was first established by the Consultative Bureau in the Xinhai year (1911), and in the first year of the Republic (1912), the Provincial Assembly agreed to levy five yuan per shi of tribute rice, divided into provincial and county taxes: four yuan for the province and one yuan for the county, or two yuan and five fen of silver per tael: one yuan and seven jiao and five fen for the province and three jiao for the county. Since the establishment of the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office, with the separation of education funds, the provincial tax of four yuan per shi of tribute rice is collected by the Finance Department for two yuan and six jiao, and the education fund receives one yuan and four jiao. The provincial tax of one yuan and seven jiao and five fen per tael of silver is collected by the Finance Department for one yuan and two jiao and eight fen, and the education fund receives four jiao and seven fen. After the Jiangsu Provincial Government approved the method of offsetting the exemption of tuition and accommodation fees for middle schools, starting from the winter tribute rice levy this year, the provincial tax of four yuan per shi of tribute rice is collected by the Finance Department for two yuan and four jiao (a decrease of two jiao compared to before), and the education fund receives one yuan and six jiao (an increase of two jiao compared to before). Although the education fund for tribute rice has increased by two jiao per shi, the actual burden on the people has not increased at all. The Jiangsu Provincial Government has repeatedly ordered the 61 counties in Jiangsu to remit two jiao more per shi for education funds starting from the winter tribute rice levy this year. This matter concerns the relief of poor children throughout Jiangsu Province, allowing them to receive secondary education free of charge, and must be implemented. The order instructs all counties not to neglect their duties. Free admission to all provincial middle schools will be implemented uniformly starting from the second semester of this year, as the winter tribute rice levy has just begun, so the fees will still be charged as usual for the autumn semester.

Wuben School to Resume Classes Tomorrow. ▲ Director Pan and Principal Yan Visited the School Yesterday to Give Instructions

The Wuben Girls' Middle School in this city has experienced unrest. Over the past few days, representatives of the faculty and staff have been persuading the students and requesting lenient treatment from the Education Bureau. The situation is gradually easing. According to reliable information obtained by reporters, the students of the school requested Director Pan Gongzhan of the Education Bureau and Principal Yan Zhenyu to visit the school in person at approximately 11:00 AM yesterday to give instructions. More than twenty grade representatives and faculty and staff representatives, including Zhu Xiangwan, Wu Jingqu, and Lu Su'an, were present. First, Director Pan gave instructions, with earnest encouragement. Then, the principal and student representatives spoke, all expressing their willingness to cooperate in the spirit of teachers and students to jointly seek the development of Wuben. A major wave has thus subsided. The Education Bureau has formally announced the approval to resume classes, and the school has also notified the parents of all students that classes will officially resume next Monday (the 20th). The announcement from the Municipal Education Bureau is recorded below:

The announcement states: This Bureau previously ordered the temporary suspension of classes at the Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School due to the fact that some students interfered with school administration and acted beyond their bounds, pending reorganization. Now, according to the report of the faculty and staff representatives of the school, they have repeatedly persuaded the students, and the students have realized their mistakes. It is appropriate to resume classes from November 20th. In addition to ordering the school to comply, this announcement is hereby made.

▲ Pan Gongzhan's Talk on Resumption of Classes. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Education Bureau of this city, issued a statement yesterday, explaining the handling of matters as follows: Wuben is the only municipal girls' middle school in this city. In recent years, the students have developed rapidly and made great progress. Therefore, I have high hopes for the future of the school. Unexpectedly, this time, due to the change of principals, the actions of some students overstepped the line, which is extremely unfortunate. My handling of this matter has been impartial. Principal Wang Xiaoying has been in charge of the school for many years, and this Bureau had no intention of transferring her. However, due to her concurrent duties, she firmly expressed her desire to resign, and attempts to retain her were unsuccessful. Therefore, this Bureau appointed Ms. Yan Zhenyu, former professor at Jinan University and Daxia University, to succeed her. Ms. Yan has served in the education sector for many years, and her scholarship and experience have always been considered rich. Having her lead Wuben is very suitable. Unexpectedly, the students were emotionally impulsive and interfered with the school administration, which is extremely regrettable. In order to protect the students' studies, I have also personally given them advice. However, some students surrounded me, intending to hold me hostage. While I cannot bear to see the students' studies neglected, I also cannot sit idly by and watch the destruction of the school spirit. After consideration, I deeply feel that reorganization is necessary. Moreover, the school order is chaotic, and the entry and exit of the gates are unchecked, which raises concerns about other accidents. Therefore, on the orders of the mayor, I temporarily ordered unarmed police officers to check entry and exit near the school gate, purely for the sake of maintaining order. Later, the faculty and staff came forward to persuade the students, urging them to realize their mistakes. I then immediately withdrew the police officers. I only seek a quick resolution to the student unrest and for the students to resume classes as soon as possible. Under the principle that students are not allowed to interfere in school administration, I have spared no effort to seek compromise in order to maintain education. Fortunately, the students have realized their mistakes, so all problems have been solved easily. The student unrest has now come to an end. I have now ordered Principal Yan and the new and old faculty and staff to quickly reorganize the school order. From the 20th, the school can resume its original state and continue classes as usual.

Artist Teng Baiye Returns to China

Mr. Teng Baiye studied sculpture and painting in Europe and the United States for ten years. He has a thorough understanding of both Chinese and Western painting theories and history. He once served as a professor at the University of Washington and was the first Chinese student to teach Western art to Westerners. Later, he received a Harvard scholarship to travel around the world to study art. In 1930, he was elected as an honorary member of the British Royal Academy of Arts. Mr. Teng's works have long been treasured by museums in Europe and the United States, and his lectures on art are also eagerly sought after by Westerners. It is reported that Shanghai University will also invite him to give a lecture soon. Mr. Teng is knowledgeable and eloquent, and his sculptures and paintings are particularly outstanding. He has now established a sculpture and painting studio in Shanghai, and the number of people seeking sculptures and paintings from him is increasing day by day. It is reported that the portraits of Zhu Baosan and Zhang Yiyun have been commissioned by their relatives and friends from Mr. Teng, and that the plaster portraits of celebrities such as Wu Jingxiong and Mao Shixun will also be made soon.

Municipal Education Bureau Rectifies Military Training in All Schools. ▲ Military Equipment Should Be Handled According to the Minimum Standards. ▲ Military Instructors May Not Appoint Others to Act as Substitutes Without Authorization.

In order to rectify military training in all schools in accordance with the Ministry's order, the Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued instructions to municipal and private senior high schools in this city, stating that military equipment should be handled according to the minimum standards and that military instructors may not appoint others to act as substitutes. The original order is recorded below:

Equipment Should Comply with Minimum Standards

The Ministry of Education's Order No. 1234 states: Approved by the Directorate General of Military Training, it is found that the Ministry previously stipulated a minimum equipment standard table in August of the 21st year of the Republic (1932), requesting notification to all schools to comply with it, as military equipment is crucial to the implementation of military education. Currently, according to reports from military instructors in various schools, most have been unable to actively procure equipment due to unspecified funding. They propose requesting a transfer of funds from various departments to facilitate the process, etc. The aforementioned is indeed the actual situation. Accordingly, we are informing you to examine this matter and to instruct the education departments of various provinces to consider handling the funding for military equipment in schools under their jurisdiction to facilitate training. We also hope to receive a reply, etc. It is hereby approved to instruct all public and private high schools and above under your jurisdiction to comply with this order, in addition to issuing an order.

Instructors Cannot Appoint Substitutes

The Ministry of Education's Order No. 11499 states: Approved by the Directorate General of Military Training, it is found that military instructors in various schools must not appoint others to act as substitutes without authorization or be absent from class arbitrarily. The Ministry has repeatedly issued orders on this matter. Currently, according to reports, some instructors in various schools still secretly and arbitrarily appoint others to act as substitutes for their duties while engaging in other activities, which is detrimental to the progress of military training. In addition to reiterating the previous order to instruct all school instructors not to request leave or be absent from their posts unless due to marriage, funerals, or major events, those who need to request leave and have been approved by submitting a report must also consult with the principal to request someone to substitute for their duties, but the term must not exceed one month, in order to emphasize their responsibilities. In addition to sending a restatement, we are notifying you to examine this matter and to inform all schools under your jurisdiction of this matter. We are issuing this order. The order to comply with this order.

Lin Sen and Others Initiate the Establishment of Huanghuagang School in Shanghai. ▲ First Run a Middle School, Then Establish a University

The martyrdom of the Huanghuagang martyrs is truly one of the most glorious pages in the history of our nation. Now, veteran members of the Tongmenghui who participated in the battle, such as Yan Deji, who is currently the director of the General Headquarters for the Suppression of Bandits, are planning to establish a Huanghuagang School in Shanghai in permanent commemoration of the martyrs. Initially, they will run junior and senior high school departments. The junior high school department will have a general studies track, and the senior high school will temporarily divide into general studies and science, business, and engineering tracks. After completing the agricultural science track, they will begin planning to establish a university. They have sought support from Chairman Lin, Chairman Chiang, President Wang, President Sun, President Yu, President Dai, as well as Zhang Ji, Niu Yongjian, Hu Hanmin, Zou Lu, Chen Lifu, Chen Zhaoying, Yang Yongtai, Zhang Qun, Wu Tiecheng, Yang Hu, Huang Fusheng, Bai Wenwei, Xu Fu, and more than twenty others to be the initiators. They are now actively preparing and looking for temporary school sites. They plan to begin enrollment in the second semester and intend to enroll at least ten free students in each grade.

"Directory of Shanghai's Large, Medium, and Small Schools" Published. ▲ Recent Investigation by Mr. Xu Wancheng

There are many primary and secondary schools in Shanghai, and it is difficult to know the exact number. Now, Mr. Xu Wancheng of the education sector in this city has spent five months compiling the "Directory of Shanghai's Large, Medium, and Small Schools." All schools in Shanghai, including cram schools, correspondence schools, and schools run by foreigners, are listed one by one, and their addresses and telephone numbers are listed in detail. It is scheduled to be published today. Mr. Xu's investigation is unprecedented. It also includes educational maxims and educational cartoons, which are profoundly meaningful. The directory is eighty pages long. Those who wish to know the development of the "quantity" of education in Shanghai must purchase and read Mr. Xu's directory. Zhongshi Bookstore on Fourth Road is the exclusive distributor. The hardcover edition is priced at one yuan, and the regular edition is priced at eight jiao. Schools that purchase it with a stamped form (sent separately by mail) will receive a 50% discount. The Shanghai education sector has never published such an investigation record, and Mr. Xu's is truly the first.

International Walking Race to Finish at Yiyuan. ▲ Agreement Has Been Reached with the Garden

The annual International Walking Race, which causes a sensation in Shanghai, will not be able to use the racecourse this year. A problem has arisen with the finish line. Last night, Mr. Murphy, the secretary of the association, stated at the hall that after the racecourse refused to continue lending its facilities for the finish line, they contacted various parties. An agreement has now been reached with the managers of Yiyuan to use the garden as the finish line.

Three-Team Sports Meet: White Rainbow, Russian Overseas Chinese, Japanese Overseas Chinese

Today at 1 PM

Gathering at Hongkou Park

Russian Overseas Chinese Include Fierce Generals

Shanghai has held an international sports meet for many years, gathering athletes from various countries to improve their skills. The meaning is good and the interest is abundant, but due to regulations, it is held only once a year. The opportunity for competition is regrettably few. Therefore, after the end of this year's international sports meet, there was a proposal to plan a private group competition. At that time, the White Rainbow Track and Field Team, the Russian Overseas Chinese Sports Association, the British Army's Argyll and Sutherland Highlanders, the Japanese Sports Association, and other groups were contacted. However, due to funding issues, it was delayed for several months. Then, it coincided with China's National Games, the Japanese athletes' selection meet, and the Russians requested a postponement to wait for the triathlon champion Anfinov. This first sports meet was delayed until 1 PM this afternoon at Hongkou Park. Unfortunately, the Argyll and Sutherland Highlanders had already left Shanghai and could not participate.

This event was originally not limited to the participation of the above-mentioned three teams, but due to limited funding and crude scale, many parties were waiting to see. Therefore, only these few participated in the first event. It is hoped that starting from the next event, Chinese and Western groups can actively participate, expanding from three teams to six or seven teams, or even more than ten teams, to create a magnificent spectacle.

The strongest supporters of this event are Mr. Shi Liangcai and Mr. Cheng Yize. Mr. Shi is responsible for the venue expenses, and Mr. Cheng generously made a large silver cup to present to the winning team. Whoever wins one event keeps it once, and whoever wins three consecutive events keeps it permanently. White Rainbow has elite soldiers and fierce generals, and is the strongest in strength, but it is heard that Cheng Jinguan, Zeng Rongzhong, Huang Shengbai, and Xu Yanbo will all be unable to attend due to other matters. The track and field situation seems to be tight, but with Zhang Jiakui's attendance in the field events, the momentum is immense. The main forces of the Japanese and Russian sides are also concentrated in the field events, so today's field event competition will definitely be exceptionally exciting.

The Russian general Anfinov's shot put has reached 14 meters, and the discus 42 meters, unrivaled in the Far East. The javelin is also more than 50 meters. Trubin's shot put exceeds 13 meters. These two are several times better than Shanghai's past champions Mutovkin. The Russian Overseas Chinese Sports Association has repeatedly telegraphed to urge them to come to Shanghai, and they may arrive today. The Japanese player Komatsu jumped 6.73 meters in the long jump last Sunday. Kuwazai's five miles is 26 minutes and 55 seconds. Based on this, the 10,000 meters is between 34 and 35 minutes. He is a strong rival to Xiaolievshenkov.

National Products Sports Committee Investigates Sports Organizations of Various Factories

Mr. Sun Daosheng, Executive Committee Member of the Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, designed and organized the National Products Industry Sports Committee. It is learned that the association plans to start with ball team competitions to arouse the interest of the national products industry. Yesterday, it specially made a form and sent it to various factories to investigate the established ball teams in order to compile statistics and promote the universal organization of subordinate factories. The original letter is recorded as follows: It is noted that Mr. Sun Daosheng, Executive Committee Member and Director of the Publicity Department of this association, designed and organized the National Products Industry Sports Committee to promote amateur sports and forge the health of employees, guiding various factories to establish football, basketball, volleyball, table tennis, and other teams, and to hold various competitions. The outstanding athletes of each team will be selected and mixed to form a national products football team, etc., to compete with the strong teams in Shanghai for the championship, thereby increasing the glory of the national products industry. This has been resolved by the first joint meeting of the 14th Executive and Supervisory Committees, and Mr. Sun, Director, has been publicly recommended to preside over the planning. Cheng Nianpeng, Gao Shiheng, Shen Guansheng, Xu Wengui, and Lin Guyun, five comrades, will assist in the progress. It is recorded. In addition to the regulations and designs made by Mr. Sun, etc., this factory has always been known for its enthusiastic promotion of sports, and its various ball teams are well-organized. Now, in order to compile statistics on the number of ball teams in national products factories, prepare schedules, so as to start the competition early, select and organize strong teams in various sports, participate in the Shanghai competition, and win the glorious championship, a survey form is enclosed accordingly. It is hoped that the established ball teams will be promptly filled out and returned within one week after the letter arrives.

Mr. Song Fuxin Presides over Qingdao Sports

Since Shen Honglie took over the Qingdao municipal administration, he has paid special attention to promoting sports. Just as Hao Gengsheng accepted the appointment of Director of Physical Education at Shandong University, he came to Qingdao with Song Fuxin, Gao Zizhen, and others. Mayor Shen greatly relied on Mr. Hao and others. On the one hand, the Education Bureau changed the organization of the Sports Committee, and on the other hand, with the promotion of Mr. Shen, the Sports Promotion Association was established to recruit sports talents in Qingdao and jointly plan the development of sports. Both associations are responsible for and presided over by Mr. Hao. After a year of efforts, Qingdao's sports have shown a vigorous atmosphere. Recently, it was heard that Mr. Hao has been appointed as a sports supervisor of the Ministry of Education and left Qingdao for Beijing. All the tasks of the Director of Physical Education and all sports organizations in Qingdao will be taken over by Song Fuxin.
